## Page 2

PREFACE:

~ Vedic astrology has been viewed by some scholars as
. polyparadigmatic, comprising of a multitude of unique schools
employing different hypothesis and independant tools for
analysis. Thus, the Parasarian system is viewed as grossly
different from that of Jaimini, Brighu or the Tajaka writers
(Neelkanthi) or even the Nadi’s (Satyanadi etc.). Consequently
much of the literature has either not surfaced for fear of un-
wanted criticism of if surfaced, is languishing for want of
serious research as scholars view the literature as "inferior"
to their system. Fortunately, due to the efforts of some brilleant
scholars Vedic astrology has come a long way from its dark
days. However, to make further progress, this science should
be viewed in a right unified perspective where the various
systems are actually parts of the whole (Vedic astrolgy).

The original Brihat parasara Hora Shastra has been sur-
facing in bits and pieces and this is evidant in every new pub-
lication which has a few more stanzas or even chapters than
the previous ones. Thus it is evidant that the original text must
have been far more voluminous that what is available now
and would have had the essence of all the systems or sub-
systems of astrology currently practised in the Indian sub-
continent, and not excluding the astrological knowledge that
migarated to China or other parts of Asia with the monks
(Buddhist, Jain etc.).

The Upadesa Sutras (Advisory stanzas) popularly called
the Jaimini Sutras were originally in eight chapters of four
quarters each and, as the name implies, were meant to supple-
ment the standard texts like Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra etc.
Maharishi Jaimini was a student of Sri Vyasa who was the
son of Parasara. So, Jaimini must have been trained in the
traditional Vedic astrology and has given these Upadesa Sutras
to bring out the finer points of astrology. Thus, many areas

---

## Page 3

like Chara and Sthira karakas (temporary/fixed significators)
that find a fleeting reference in the standard texts are explained
in detail. Similarly while Jaimini has dealt with seventy phalita
dasas and fourteen Ayur dass he has generally avoided the
constellation based dasa (excepting Lagna kendradi Rasi
Dasas or Sudasa) asking the reader to refer to standard texts.
(1 have explained as many dasas as possible in this transla-
tion and a detailed exposition will require a seperate book).
Again, Jaimini asks the reader to refer to standard texts for
the divisional charts while explaining only those like
Saptamsa, Rudramsa, Shastamsa etc which do not find ad-
equate coverage elsewhere. My interpretation is on the basis
of my learning and any error is attributable only to my own
inattentiveness, for which, the erudite readers may kindaly
 . enlighten me.

In the determination of (monthly) signinficators for the
, period of gestation, most standard texts give the natural
significators Jaimini gives the fixed significatoors besides add-
ing a novel method of timing events during pregnancy. Even
the use of Varnada Lagna in the epoch chart is meant to supple-
ment standard texts. These can also be successfully used in
horary charts or the natal saptamasa chart D-7) of the par-
ents. Perhaps the only area where he has differed is the delin-
eation of body parts. By explaining in detail the use of such
sensitive special ascendants like the Hora Lagna etc, Jaimini
has taken Vedic astrology to unprecedented heights which
no serious scholar can afford to miss. For example, it is tradi-
tionally known that the second Lord in the twelfth house is a
specific combination for poverty and it is found in the chart
‘of Queen Victoria! However, Jaimini teaches that the Varnada
Lagna in the second house is good for power and position.
This is found in the chart of the Queen and the results of
"second Lord in twelfth house" get modified to "Lord of
Varnada lagna in the eleventh house from it" thereby result-

---

## Page 4

ing in a dhanyog (wealth & prosperity). The traditionalists
view of Vedic astrology as a unified whole is advocated and |
to the extent feasible I have given quotes from standard texts.

While a flawless commentary by the brilliant Neelkanth
15 available on the first two chapters the third chapter, at least
in the available sanskrit works, 15 in an uncorrelated manner
showing that in the process of transfer by word of mouth some
order was lost. These have been arranged (only in Chapter ITI
'Quarter3) on the basis of my learning and it is possible that
those who are more erudite may like to advise me further on
this. I shall be most obliged for their valuable suggestions.
. While this book should suffice, research scholars can consult
- the bibliography for further reading. 1 do not claim that the
Jaimini Sutras are complete as the last four chapters are not
available and will have to be added subsequently, if at all
. they are traced. While reading these stanzas the readeris cau-
tioned against taking a hard line attitude without actuallly
trying out their applicability. Again, there should be no fixa-
tion for names as 'Chara dasa’ is quite different from 'chara
Paryaya dasa’ etc.

Jaimini has explained a novel method of determining
the sex of the child on the basis of the vighati (Birth time)
from Sunrise or Sunset and this can also be used for rectify-
ing horoscopes. Instead of going into all the important com-
bination which are available in standard texts, Jaimini has
just explained a few. The explanation of the Shakti Yoga gives
a new insight into understanding these combinatious.

Explanatory notes and illustration have been provided
to bring out the applicability of the stanzas which have been
. specifically refered to in the explanation to charts. It is hoped
that this work meets with the expectations of the learned as-

` trologers.

Words would not suffice to appreciate the efforts and

---

## Page 5

inspiration provided by close elder astrologers.
.Vedicastrology is indebted to the Sagar family for patronising
publication of various books over the past few generations
‘now and I express my gratitude to Sri Narinder Sagar for his
advise and expertise in the publication of this book. God will-
ing, we should be able to throw more light on Vedic Astroi- `
-ogy in the future as well .

I prostrate at the Lotus feet of Sri Sri Jagannath of Puri
'(Orissa), my Gurus and my parents for their blessings.

New Delhi 18/8/97 ~~. Sanjay Rath

Chapter I Quarter 1

` 1.1.1. उपदेश व्याख्यास्यामः॥
~The explanatory verses (that will from the key in
deciphering the Jaimini Sutras) are being initiated.

All ancient Sanskrit works were always initiated with
a benedictory address and in this stanza, the sage pays
obeisance at the feet of Sri Visnu (पः is the middle letter
of ‘Aum’) for the benefit of mankind

Note : (i) At the outset the reader is cautioned that the
Jaimini Sutras are often couched with multiple meanings and
at places the best of commentators havc held divergent opin-
ions. Thus *upadesam’ is also read as ‘u’-‘Pace’- ‘Sam’ where

represents Sri Visnu, ‘Pade’ means ‘fect’ and ‘Sam’ means
‘for general welfare

(11) Jaimini has been following the ‘katapayadi’ varga
system of numerology for coding the number of the houses
and signs within words. In this system, the sanskrit
vowels have a zero value and each of the consonants
Ka, Ta, Pa & Ya have a numerical value of one, hence
- the name Katapayadi Varga. The consonants following these
have a sequentially higher numerical value as per Table 1.1.

Write the word of the stanza in devanagari script
and remove the ‘matras’ and incomplete/half letters. The
numerical value of the remaining letters should be written
“sequentially and the number so obtained should be re-
versed. Divide this by 12. The reminder gives the sign/
house referred to in the stanza. For example, the word
"Dara, has two full letters 'da’, and 'ra’, of numerical value
8, & 2, respectively. Thus, dara in 82, which reversed
gives 28. Now, 28 divided by 12 leaves a reminder of 4.
Hence, ‘dara’, would mean the fourth house or the fourth
sign i.e. Cancer, depending on the contcxi.

1.1.2. अभिपश्यन्ति ऋक्षाणि, पाशर्वभे =
The signs in the zodiac aspect those facing it
while the signs juxtaposed cannot be aspected.

Notes: The Zodiacal diagram referred to is currently
in vogue in South India. From Aries, every fourth sign is
sequentially, movable, fixed or dual. A movable sign is
aspected by and aspects all fixed signs except the one
juxtapose. A fixed sign is aspected by and aspects all

the special aspect see fig 1.3. ।

. *] Arrows indicate signs having mutual facial/aspect.

*2 A simpler memory aide is that the facial aspect is
always to a sign also owned by its Lord except in the
case of luminaries and Satur. Thus, Pisces and Sag-
ittarius render facial aspect to each other as both are
ruled by Jupiter. The exceptions are the Leo-Capri-
con and Cancer-Aquarius pair. All these pairs are
also called 'sammukha rasi

1.1.3, तत्रिष्ठाश्च तद्वत्‌।

The aspect of the planets is the same as the signs
they are stationed in.

Notes: Readers would be aware of the natural aspect
` of planets employed in vedic astrology. These aspects are
called Grahadristi or Planetary sight. According to the

present stanza the planets tend to aspect as per their sign
position. Thus, a Jupiter in Pisces will aspect Gemini,
Virgo and Sagitarius. This is Rasi Dristi or Signs sight
and is not unique to the Jaimini school as has been made

` . out. Parasara has also given a detailed exposition of Rasi

drishti in his monumental classic Brihat Parasara Hora
Shastra. -

signs in the second (Bhagya = 14/12 = 2 Rem), fourth
(Dara = 28/12 = 4 Rem) and eleventh. (Shoola =35/12=11

intervene in its affairs. :

` , 1.1.5. कामस्था भूयसा पापानाम्‌॥ |
। Malefic Signs/Planets in the third house from a sign
, (or planet) also intervene in its affairs (or cause argala).

Note : Kama = 51/12 = रछा. (०.०८)

1.1.6 रिफ नीच कामस्था विरोधिनः॥
| The Signs (or planets) in the tenth, twelfth or third
` from a sign (or planet) obstruct the argala

Notes: Stanza 1.1.6 should be read after stanza
` 1.1.4 Rifa = 22/12 = 10 Rem; Neecha = 60/12 = 12 Rem;
Kama = 51/12 = 3 Rem

Argala is the intervention brought about by signs
and/or planets in the 2nd, 4th or 110 from a sign (or
planet). This intervention tends to promote the affairs
ruled by the sign (or planet) by fair or foul means
depending on the nature of the signs and planets involved.
This intervention in the 2nd, 4th or 11th house is ob-
structed by the signs (or planets) in the 12th, 10th or 3rd
house respectively. The rider at stanza 1.1.5 implies that
malefics in the third house, while simultaneously obstruct-
ing the intervention in the 11th house, also themselves
cause argala {or intervene).

1.1.7. नं न्यूना विबलाश्च॥
The Strength of the intervention (argala) and its
` obstruction should be assessed to determine prevalence.

Notes: The strengths of signs have been dealt with in
` Chapter II Quarter 3

The signs/planets in the fifth house cause interven-
-tion which is obstructed by the signs/planets in the ninth
house - : SE ` `

Notes: The intervention of the fifth house is second-
ary as compared to the 2nd, 4th, & 1111 houses. The fifth
house in obstructed by the ninth house.

1.19. विपरीतं केतोः॥

In the case of Ketu (or the sign occupied by
- Ketu), the argala reckoning is done in the reverse
direction.

»

ह Notes: The counting of the 2nd, 4th and other
houses that intervene in .the affairs of Ketu (or the
sign dispositing Ketu) in done in the reverse so also, the
signs obstructing these interventions are reckoned in the

"reverse.

1.1.10. आत्माधिाकः कलादिभिर्नभोगः सप्तानामष्टमान्यं वा।
ः The planet which obtains the highest longitude
= (irrespective of signs) is the atmakaraka (soul) in the
` seven or eight planet charakaraka (temporal signifactor)
scheme.

Notes: The stanzas 1.1.10-19 explains the scheme
of temporary significators (charakaraka) which is differ-
ent from the natural significations (naisargika Karaka).
, Karaka means doer or significator and 'atma' means the
"5001. Thus the atmakaraka represents the 'soul' of the
horoscope. There are two schemes in determining
Charakarakas. One that considers the seven planets from
the Sun to Saturn and the other that includes Rahu
, Jaimini has accepted the existance of both schemes but
has recommended the eight planet scheme

Again, in the eight planet scheme, some astrologers
hold that the longitude of Rahu alone should be reckoned
from the end of the sign it occupies, while others consider
this for all retrograde planets.

---

## Page 17

Chapter I Quarter I 7

Parasara : HASTE सम्प्रवक्षयानि ग्रहानात्मादिकारकान।
सप्तख्यादिशन्यन्तान शहवन्तान वाडष्टसंख्यान।।
अशेः समौग्नहो द्रौ चेद्शदवन्तान्‌ चिन्तयेत्‌ यदा।

| सप्तैव कारकानेवं केचिदष्यै प्रचक्षते।।

Parasara accepts the existance of two schools of
‘thought using the seven and eight planets for temporary
signification (charakaraka). While those advocating the
seven planet scheme bring in Rahu only when two planets
` obtain the same longitude (irrespective of signs), others
always include Rahu in the eight planet charakaraka
scheme.

Parasara : आत्मा सूर्यदिखेटाना मध्ये हमशाधिको ग्रहः।
अंशासम्ये कलाधिक्यान्‌ तत्साम्ये विकलाधिकः।
` बुधै राशिकलाधिक्याद ग्राह्यो नैवत्मकारकः।
अंशाधिकः कारकः स्यादल्प भागोडन्त्यकारकः।
मध्यांशो मध्वश्वेतः स्यादुपश्वेट स एवं हि।
विलोमगमनाद्राहोरंशा शोध्याः खवहिनतः।।

The planet with the highest longitude (degrees) in a
sign qualifies for the Afmakaraka. If the degrees of two
planets are identical, then the minutes, and if the minutes
are identical, then the seconds of arc traversed should be
considered for declaring the Atmakarak. (This tussle for
Karakatwa could occur among the lower significators as
well ie. two or more planets could contend for the
, Bhratrukarak or other signification. In all such cases the
comparision should be made upto the seconds of arc). The
planets which fails to qualify are also called Antyakarak,
Madhyakheta or upakheta. The longitude of Rahu is reck-
oned from the end of the sign ie. 30° minus actual
longitude.

1.1.11. § 32 . बन्धामोक्षयोः॥

The Atmakaraka indicates the (वद्वि (souls guid-
ing deity) and its disposition indicates bondage (of the
soul ie. rebirth) or emancipation (moksha).

Notes :
Parasara : आत्मख्यारकस्तेषु प्रधानं कथ्येते द्विज |
एवं जातकाधीशो विज्ञेयो द्विजसत्तम |
यथा भूगो प्रसिद्धोडस्ति नराणां क्ितिपालकः।
सर्ववार्ताधिकारी च बन्धकृन्मोक्षक्रत्‌ तथा |

The Atmakaraka enjoys a pre-eminent position among
| “the planets and represents divinity in the horoscope (i.e.
~ the Ista Devata in the Hindu tradition). It is the controller

of all the affairs of the native and the sustainer, like a
king, deciding and guiding the affairs of his subjects. Its
disposition in to be examined for bondage & liberation
(i.e. emancipation).

` Parasara: यथा राजाज्ञया विप्र! पुत्रमात्यादयो जना: |
ः समर्था लोककार्येषु तथेवान्येपि कारकाः | |

आत्मानुकूलमेवात्र भवन्ति फलदायकः।
प्रतिकूले यथा भूपे सर्वे अमात्यादयो द्विज! || `
कार्य कर्तुं मनुष्याणं न समर्था भवन्ति हि।
तथाडडत्मकारकं कृरे नाडन्ये स्वशुभदायकः। |
अनुकूले नृपे यद्रत्‌ सर्वेडमात्यादयो द्वित ||
नाशुभ Fad दद्वनान्ये स्वाशुभदायकः। |

Just like a king the धारा ८६, has a preeminent posi-
tion (vis-a-vis other karaka planets) in the horoscope. Like

---

## Page 19

Chapter 1 Quarter I ~ ** 9

the activities of men, the atmakaraka should be in agreement
for success in every activity. The results, benefic or malefic,
will largely depend on the aimakaraka. If the other planets
forbode evil and the afmakaraka in favourable, the intensity
of the evil in greatly reduced. Similarly if the other planets
indicate excellent results and the armakaraka in unfavourable,
success is elusive and negative results well be felt.

1.1.12. तस्यानुसरणादमात्यः।
The planet obtaining the next (second) highest longi-
tude is called the Amatyakaraka (Minister).

1.1.13. तस्य भ्राता
The planet obtaining the next (third) highest longi-
tude is called the Bhratrukaraka (co-born).

1.1.14. तस्य माता `
` The planet obtaining the next (fourth) highest longi-
tude is called the Matrukaraka (Mother)

. 1.1.15. तस्य पिता। |
The planet obtaining the next (fifth) highest longitude
is called the Pitri Karaka (Father).

` 1.1.16. तस्य पुत्रः।
The Planet obtaining the next (sixth) highest longi-
tude in called the Puirakarak- (child).

1.1.17. तस्य॒ ज्ञातिः।
. The planet obtaining the next (seventh) highest longi-
tude is called the Gnatikaraka (Relative).

1.1.18. तस्य दारास्च। |

The planet obtaining the next (eighth) highest longi-
, tude (i.e. the lowest longitude) is called the Darakarak
~ (spouse)

## Page 20

10 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

. Notes : (i) it is evident from Stanzas 1.1.10-18 that
Jaimini also favoured the eight planet Charakaraka scheme
“like his illustrious predecessor Parasara. In the Brihat
Parasara Hora Shastra, after indicating the eight Karakas,
Parasara adds -मातृकारकमेवाऽन्ये वदन्ति सुतकारकम्‌' ie. some
(other) astrologers use the seven planet charakarak scheme
where the Matrukarak and Putrakarak are one and the
same. Thus, they avoid Rahu and the Putrakaraka. The
implication is that neither of the two great savants of
Vedic Astrology agreed to this seven planet scheme. So

` this may be dispensed with

(ii) What happens if two or more planets attain the
same longitude?
Parasara : द्वौ ग्रहो भागतुल्यौ चेर्जायेतां यस्य जन्मनि |
तदग्रकारकस्यैव लोपो ज्ञेयो द्विजोत्तम |

स्थिरकारकवशात्तस्य फलं ज्ञेयं शुभाडशुभम्‌ | |

If two planets attain the same longitude, then they
become the Karaka jointly i.e. both are to be examined for
purposes of signification. The next slot falls vacant and is
to be filled by the natural significator. For example, if
after the Bhratrukarak (Co-born), two planets attain the
same longitude, they both become Matrukarakas (Moth-
ers). The next slot of Pifrukaraka (father) falls vacant and
1s to be studied from the natural significator for father i.e.
the Sun. If instead, three planets having the same longi-
tude became Matrukarakas (Mothers), the next two slots
of Pitrikarak (father) and Putrakarak (son) would fall
vacant and the Sun and Jupiter respectively would have to
take these places, being the natural significators.

charakaraka scheme (excluding Rahu) in which the
Matrikarak and Putrakarak are merged.

1.1.27. न क्वचित्‌
There are exceptions (to the rule vide preceding
stanzas) \

५

Note : What are the exceptions and in which cases
are they applicable? the exceptions to the general rules
vide stanzas 1.1.25 & 26 have been explained by Parasara
as follows :-

(i) The exceptions are the fixed signs Taurus,
Leo, Scorpio and Aquarius. Taurus and Scorpio are
even, yet the count is zodiacal while Leo and Aquarius
are odd and yet the count is reverse. Then the signs
having zodiacal count are called vimsopada (odd footed)
and the signs with reverse count are called sampada(even
footed).

(i1) If the Lord is exalted, a year is added and if
debilitated, a year is subtracted

(iii) Rahu- and Saturn are the Lords of Aquarius
while Ketu and Mars are the Lords of Scorpio

(a) If both Co-Lords are in the sign, it contrib-
utes 12 years (e.g. If Ketu and Mars are in
| Scorpio, it gives 12 years).

(b) If one is placed elsewhere, determine the
period from this separately placed co-lord. (If
-Ketu is in Scorpio and Mars in Aries, the dasa
should be reckoned through Mars. Counting
from Scorpio to Ares, we have six signs,
minus one gives 5 years).

(€) If both are placed in different signs, the
` stronger shall determine the dasa.

(0) If both are equally strong, the larger period
should be adopted

1.1.28. नाथान्ताः समाः प्रायेण

Normally, the count (as obtained in the preceding
stanzas) gives the dasa period of the sign in years.

Notes : What are the exceptions? The dasa period
in years is used for natal (human) horoscopy. This will
require suitable modifications for other charts depending
-on the Paramayus (full longivity) of the chart. For ex-
. ample, in a horary chart concerning the swearing-in of a
। government, the maximum dife of the Lok Sabha (House
of People in India) is 5 years. Then the dasa periods 'P'
would have to be proportionately reduced by the formula
Px5+120

1.1.29. यावद्धिवेकमावृत्तिरभानाम्‌॥
Every dasa has 12 equal antardasas of the twelve
signs

Note : (Viveka = 144/12 = 12 Rem). Thus, if the
dasa of a sign is for 7 years, each of the 12 antardasas is
for 7 months

1.1.30. याववीशाश्रयं पदमूक्षाणाम्‌॥

The arudha (Pada Lagna) of the Ascendant (and other
signs) is the sign obtained by counting as many signs
from the Lord as it has progressed from the ascendant (or
‘other sign)

Notes : For example, if Mars is in Virgo for Aries
` ascendant, we have six signs counting from Aries to
Virgo. Now counting six signs from Virgo, we arrive at
। Aquarius which in the Arudha (Image) or Pada lagna. In
this manner the Arudhas (Images) of the 12 signs can be

determined. For Aduarlus, amongst Satu &_Fal Aquarius, amongst Saturn & Rahu and

many signs from this house.

in the 1st or 7th houses. If the Arudha computed as per

to be determined. The longitude of Rahu should be sub-
tracted from 30° for this purpose.

The next step is to write the Charakaraka Chakra
(Temporary significator chart) by arranging the eight plan-
ets in a hierarchy of decreasing longitudes.

Leo and the lord of the ascendant, viz. the Sun. is in the
~ ascendant. Hence the Arudha is in the tenth house Taurus.
Again, Scorpio, the fourth house has two lords Ketu and
Mars. Both are unconjoined. Ketu in Capricorn is aspected
by the five planets in Leo including Jupiter and Mercury
‘whereas Mars in Virgo is aspected only by Saturn. Capri-
‘corn with Ketu is stronger. Hence counting from Scorpio to
Ketu we have 3 signs and similarly, the third house from
Ketu, viz Pisces becomes the Matripada (IV). Similarly,
Aquarius is the seventh house having two Lords Saturn and
Rahu. Saturn has the advantage of the aspect of Mars as
well as placement in a dual sign thereby determining the
Darapada (VII) at Libra.

In a similar manner, the Arudhas of the planets are
also determined. The luminaries and the nodes own one
sign each. This makes the job easy. For example, the Sun
is in Leo and the pada is temporarily in Leo. Since this is
not allowed, the tenth sign Taurus becomes the Arudha of
the Sun. Similarly for Mars-Aries, Venus-Libra, Mercury-
Virgo, Jupiter-Pisces and Saturn-Capricorn determines the
Arudhas. These have been shown in Fig. 1.6. Readers
may refer to Stanza 2.3.5-2..3.17 for sources of strength of

KARTA : Any planet aspecting/joining the Janma
Lagna, Hora lagna or Ghatika lagna is the Rasi,
Drekkara or Navamsa charts is a Karta. Some as-

` trologers add that the aspect could also be to the

seventh house from these ascendants for a planet to

` qualify as Karta. However, the seventh house rules

spouse and a planet aspecting the seventh houses

from either of the three lagnas in either of the three

charts does become a Karta for spouse. Similarly for

' , the other houses, the Karta's can be ascertained.

(b)

KEVALA : If the Subhapati (Lord of Moon sign)
aspect/joins the Janma lagna (or Hora/Ghatika lagna)
it is termed as Kevala. If the Kevala aspects both of
Janma lagna and Hora lagna ‘or Janma lagna and
Ghatika lagna it is called Kevala Yogada. If the
Kevala aspects all three of Janma, Hora and Ghatika
lagnas, it is called a Kevala mahayogada.

For example, in chart 1 (Fig. 1.7) the Moon is in Leo
and the Lord of Moon sign, the Sun is in Janma Lagna
(Leo) conjoins Hora lagna (Leo) land aspects Ghatika
Lagna (Libra). Hence, the Sun is a Kevala Mahayogada.
Rajiv Gandhi was born with a silver spoon and lived a
life of plenty with Rajyoga as well. These are the results
of good karma in the past birth.

Similarly, six planets except Rahu, Mars & Saturn
qualify as Karta’s in Rasi chart. Rahu qualifies in
Navamsa while Saturn and Mars qualify in Drekkana.
All eight planets except Saturn qualify as Swakarta
(aspecting/joining Janma lagna in the Rasi, Navamsa

` & Drekkana): Similarly planets aspecting/joining

Hora lagna become Dhanakarta (wealth) and planets
aspecting/joining Ghatika lagna become Rajkarta
(power/authority).

---

## Page 33

(©)

Chapter 1 Quarter I ` 23

YOGADA: Yoga means Union and a planet
aspecting/conjoining the Janma and Hora lagna or
Janma lagna and Ghatika lagna becomes a yogada
(ie. capable of taking the native to ‘prosperity or
power respectively). It is important to note that’ the
planet must aspectfjoin the natal ascendant for the
native to himself enjoy the wealth and position. If the
yogada aspect/join only the Hora langa and ghatika

"lagna, wealth & power will be with somebody else
~ he associates with.

In the illustration, there are six yogada in the Rasi
chart itself and that too, all the natural benefics and
the luminaries. The natural malefics Saturn, Mars and
Rahu have stayed out. Five of the six yogada aspéct

all three of Janma, Hora and Ghatika lagna. The

native was the eldest son of the longest reigning
Prime Minister of India and was associated (directly
or indirectly) with the topmost level of government.

DIVISIONAL CHARTS: The construction of: divi-
sional chart can be studied from standard text like
Brihat Parasana Hora Shastra Most astrologers use
three charts namely the Rasi (D1), Navamsa (D9) and
Drekkana (D3) Charts.

(A) DREKKANA RECKONING: There are two
methods of reckoning the drekkanas i.e. by either
regular count (zodiacal/reverse) or triplicity. In the
method based on regularity, the Parivrittitraya

+ Drekkana (based on Vriddha Karika) uses a zodiacal

` count while the Somanath Drekkana uses zodiacal

count only for odd signs and reverse for even signs.
In the method based on triplicity, Parasara Drekkana
takes the trines from the sign itself while the Jagannath
Drekkana takes the trines from the movable sign. The
method of Parasara (table 1.13) is recommended.

(b) NAVAMSA RECKONING : The method of reck-

oning navamsa occupied by the ascendant and

"the planets as taught by Parasara (Table 1.15) is widely

-accepted. These are regular and Zodical. Some astrologers

use the Phalaratnamala whereby the reckoning of navamsas,

although regular for odd signs, is the reverse for even
signs. This is not recommended.

(ध) HORA RECKNING: Readers will be familiar

with the Parasara Hbra (D2) reckoning whereby the first

` hora (0-15°) of an odd sign and the second hora (15-30°)

of an even sign is ruled by the sun. Similarly, the second

hora of an odd sign and the first hora of an even sign ‘are

, ruled by the moon. (Table 1.16). Some astrologers use the

among astrologers regarding Swamsa. For the present
"Swamsa" should be understood as the navamsa of lagna |
[and other planets (karakas)]. The navamsa sign occupied
. by the atmakarak 13. called the Farakamsa in the Navamsa |
chart. Similarly, the navamsa sign occupied by the lagna |
is called lagnamsa. 'Swa' generally refers to lagna and in |
its broader sense, includes the atmakaraka. |

the desire of the soul. If the two conjoin, the stage is set

Notes : (i) Stanzas 14-22 indicates the vocation and
were directly applicable in the days of Jaimini when
“vocational diversification was negligible and life was quite
simple. However, the basic principles hold good even
today. The Sun indicates government/political work while
venus indicates working in big bureaucracies in the
private sector. Ketu no longer. uses elephants to carry
loads (at least very rarely) and huge diesel trucks and
other transport vehicles have come to stay. In a subse-
. quent stanza Jaimini indicates watch repairing under Ketu
.and this maybe extended to computers and other delicate
working devices.

ह (ii) In actual practise very few horoscopes will indi-
` cate professional direction in the Karakamsa. This 15 due
to the fact that the Atmakarak is the soul and the

Karakamsa planets indicate the desire of the soul. Every-

body does not achieve this. The lagnamsa indicates that
, which is easily obtained by the native and is-a better
indicator of the vocation/abilities. However, the dasamsa

(D-10) holds the key to the career & professional achieve:

ments and is beyond the scope of this book.

1.2.22 (0) शुक्र दृष्टौ विशेषण

` 1.2.29 स गुलिके विषदो विषहत्तो वा॥

Gulika in Swamsa makes the native consume poison

-0 poison others.

Note : (i) Various drugs and psychotropic substances

‘are consumed by ignorant/misled people who are bound

by its addiction. If Mars conjoin/aspects, the native sells
or administers these drugs while Jupiters aspect/conjunc-
tion indicates self consumption. The aspect of Venus or

the Sun cures the evil or prevents its occurance.

(ii) Gulika is an upagraha and is called the child of
saturn. The day duration is divided into 8 parts (called
Yama) and, begining from the weekday lord, in the
sequence of the days of the week, each planet owns one
part. The eighth part is owned by Gulika. Thus, Gulika is
the ascendant for the time ending the part ruled by saturn.
For example on a Wednesday (day birth), saturn owns the
4th part. If the day duration was exactly 12 hours and the
Sunrise at exactly 6 a.m., Gulika would rise at the end of
the fourth part i.e. 12 x 4/8 = 6 hrs after sunrise or 12:00
Noon. Table (1.19) gives the ready reckoner for calculat-
ing Gulika. The additional inforation required would be
the Sunrise/Sunset and Day/Night duration depending on

day/night birth.

---

## Page 48

38 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

aturn for 12 hr
night

Let us take a hypothetical case of birth on a Thurs-
day, Sun Rise : 5:42" am. and day Duration Hr 12:36".
Time of Gulika rising = S.R. + [(4:30") x Day Duration’) +12]

= (5:42) + [(4:30") x (12:36) +12]
= 10:25 : 30" am

Now determine the ascendant for the place for birth
at 10: 25:30” a.m. This is Gulika.

.aspects the third house thereby making the native passion-

“dient person while also saying that a benefic in the Sth

ers & elders! is contradictory. Hence the version given by
this scribe may be accepted.

Sun to Saturn are Agwi, Jala, Skanda (Kartikeya), Visnu,

with a host of Gods and demi-gods.

EXPLANATORY NOTES & CASE STUDIES

1. SWAMSA : In Stanza 1.2.1 I have preferred the
.broad interpretation of results of the various navamsas on
the basis of the ascendant and planets instead of restrict-
ing it to Karakamsa alone. The results indicate in the
subsequent stanzas are generally negative and this need
‘not always apply to the Karakamsa as will be seen in
‘actual practise. In fact ‘Grahanam’ covers the planets and
the results (negative) of the navamsas of those planets
inclined to indicate evil results should be studied.

(a) Badhak : It is the lord of obstruction. For a
movable sign, the eleventh house, the ninth house for a
fixed sign and the seventh house for a dual sign are the
places of obstruction (Badhak sthana). The Lord of the
badhaksthana from the ascendant shall surely be included
to damage the health. -

Chart 2 : Male born 7.8.1963, at. 21:14 at 21१ 28
84 E 01

(Virgo) is the badhaksthana. The Lord of this house
(Mercury) is placed in Leo in the navamsa chart indicating
the danger of bites from dogs and other canines (Stanza
1.2.6). In February 1969 the native was severely bitten by
a dog. The Narayana Padakrama Dasa-antar was Pisces-
Leo and the Vimsottari Dasa-antar was Jupiter-Mercury.
The Karakamsa is Virgo and Lagnamsa is Scorpio and
neither has indicated the result. Thus, we may infer that
the negative results of Navamsa should be studied from
the evil planets like Badhak lord etc.

afflict the putrakarak thereby denying progeny. However,
Jupiter gave him an excellent disciple (also seen from 5th
house and putrakarak; Swami Vivekananda, who was born
11 Saggitarius Lagna of Jupiter) spread his teachings
throughout the world and founded the Ramakrishna Mission.

Jaimini has taught that the spiritual diety is to be
seen from (1) the 12th house from Atmakarak (2) the
sixth house from Amatyakarak and (3) the Bhratrukarak.
The twelfth (emancipation) from Karakamsa is the sym-
bolic world to which the soul departs and hence, is the
place of Atma Gyana or Gyanayoga (the yoga of knowl-
edge). The sixth (service) from Amatyakarak shows the
Karmayoga (yoga of Action) and also shows the sustainer

## Page 84

24 । . Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

in the present world. The Bhratrukarak shows Bhakti or
the undying attachment of the heart. In the navamsa the
Karakamsa is Capricorn with the Sun in the 12th house in
-Saggitarius. The Sun represents Lord Siva and Saggitarius
` shows His form as the teacher. Sri Ramakrishna’s tutelary

diety and the sage of soul was Sri Dakshineswara
(form of Lord Sibu १ the teacher) and Satyaloka, respec-

thereform is again Saggitarius with the Sun in it indicating
that his sustenance (both physical and spiritual) will be
done by Sri Dakshineswasa and his Karma yoga that leads
to undying fame shall be brought about by the Sun is

Saggitarius. It is indeed noteworthy that Swami Viveka-

, nanda was born in Saggitarius ascendant with the Sun. In
fact, Ramakrishna Paramhansa used to say that in Swami
Vivekananda he saw the Lord Siva. Is it a mere

Charts 9 & 10 belong to two twins born about 2 minutes
apart. Most astrologers who ignore the vargas would be at.
pains to explain as to how the lives of these two twins are so
different. The Rasi chart is exactly identical and so are
Aroodhas, Chara karakas etc. However, the Navamsa lagna
has changed. Chart 9 has Sagittarius navamsa ascending as
Chart 10 has Capricorn navamsa ascending

Satyam (Chart 9 Navamsa) is a brilliant student (Jupiter
and Mercury in the fifth house), and is very optimistic
(Saggitarius rising). His childhood days were spent with his
। maternal grandmother (Venus aspects amsa lagna).

He is brave (Mars & Ketu in the 6th house) But is not
very good in science. He is good in commerce and accoun-
tancy (Merceury in Sth house) and has a jobe as an accoun-
tant. The Atmakarak (Venus) is in a quadrant and aspects the
ascendant, and the lord of ascendant (Jupiter) is in the elev-
enth from it. The sun also aspects the ascendant (he has a
receding hair line and good eyesight). Both the Sun & Venus
so placed ensure good health and a jovial & amicable dispo-
sition

Shivam (Chart 10- Navamsa) is a mediocre student (Mars
& Ketu in the 5th - except mathematics) and was more inter-
ested in games. The Atmakarak (Venus ) is in the 6th house
and the lagnesh (Saturn) is in the sixth from Karakamsa. He
is of very poor health having kidney stones and various other
problems. Mars (also as 4th Lord) aspects the ascendant to
show his childhood days with mother. With Capricorn rising
in navamsa, he is a skeptic and has little belief in astrology or

such areas instead, always wanting 'rational' (bounded!) ex-
planations. He has weak Sight as the Sun and Venus aspect
the twelfth and is sombre and serious (Saturn & Rahu aspect
the ascendant).

The following inferences can be arrived at from these
charts:-

(1) The navamsa chart holds the key to deciphering the
horoscope and is an indispensable tool.

nounced results,

caused by the other significations of the planets. For ex-

enemies or the sun in service etc. The other indications of
planets can be had from standard texts.

and spouse) (a) If the darapada is in a quadrant or trine

(around the time of marriage), but the couple are not
physically compatible. (c) If the darapada is in the third or
eleventh from Arudha lagna , finances will be poor but
there will be physical harmony in marriage.

1.3.26. तेष्वेकस्मिन्‌ न्यूने FAH

If either one or two of the lagna, hora lagna or ghatika
lagna or the seventh houses is not aspected by the (yogada)
planet, the Rajyoga is reduced proportionately.

Notes : For a powerful Rajyoga the lagna, hora Lagna
and ghatika lagna (or their seventh house) should be
: aspected by one planet. If the planet fails to aspect either
one of the three, 106 Rajyoga is reduced and if it fails to -
. aspect/ join two of the three ascendants, the Rajyoga is
even weaker ।

1.3.27. एवमंशतो दृक्काणतेश्च॥

The above rules of reduction (in the preceding stanza)
is applicable to the evaluation of the Rajyogas in Navamsa
and Drekkana charts as well.

Note : (i) A perfect Rajyoga requires aspect to the
ascendant, Hora Lagna and Ghatika lagna in either of Rasi
~ Navamsa or Drekkana charts. The fever aspects to two or
one special ascendant reduces the Rajyogé. ‘This is to be
~ seen in the Navamsa and Drekkana charts as well. How-
ever, a perfect Rajyoga in the Rasi charf is far more
effective than in a Navamsa or Drekkana chart. Similarly,
if two or more planets become yogadas, the Rajyoga is
proportionately strengthened.

(ii) Parasara mentions the use of Navamsa and
Drekkana charts for spouse and co-boms respectively. How-
ever, most astrologers use these two charts in addition to
. the Rasi chart for evaluating the entire horoscope. Readers
may refer to the Explanatory notes after chapter I quarter 1
for more information

(iii) The following ‘points should also be borne in

---

## Page 96

86 * Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
mind while evaluating the Rajyoga:

(a) The strength of the yogada planet like being in
exaltation, moolatrikona etc. or being involved in
other yogas like parivartan (exchange of signs)
or such other combinations.

(b) The nature of the yogada and the nature of plan-
ets aspecting the yogada. The aspect of the sun
gives moral fibre and character. The aspect of the

moon ensures reputation, mental strength and
good will. The aspect of mars gives daring and
physical strength. The aspect of mercury gives
oratorical abilities and friends and relatives. The
aspect of jupiter gives wisdom and learning while
that of venus gives good looks and luxuries. The
aspect of saturn gives servants. The aspect of
` वीप gives foreign associates while that of ketu
gives beflicose companions.

If jupiter is the yogada, Rajyoga comes through

' the elevation of others or voluntary renunciation
‘by the superior while saturn causes a downfall of
the superiors. Rahu gives Rajyoga by causing a
scandal and spoiling the reputation of others while
ketu may cause a revolt, rebellion or war. Mars
will surely destroy the health of the competition.
In this manner, the effects of the yogada, aspects
and argalas on the yogada should be analysed.

(c} Unless the yogada is supported by the sun, the
Rajyogas cannot be initiated and unless sup-

, ported by the Moon the same cannot be sus-
tained. Without the luminaries support, some yoga
effects will be felt during the period of the yogada.

1.3.32. पित लाभाधिपाच्चैवम्‌॥. `

0) The sign occupied by the lord of the ascendant is

Similarly the sign occupied the Lord of Arudha Lagna is

the seventh from Arudha lagna is called Paka Arudha
Saptama. If benefics occupy the 2nd, 4th, 5111 8th and 9th

1.3.33. मिश्रे समाः॥
Mixed planets reduce the Rajyoga

Note : Benefics should be in the 2nd, 4th, 511, 8th &
Oth houses while malefics should be in the 3rd & 6th
houses. If both benefics and malefics are present, the
Rajyoga is (proportionately) reduced. :

1.3.34. दरिद्रो विपरीते

If malefics are in the 2nd, 4th, 5th, 8th or 9th houses
as benefics are in the 3rd & 6th houses, poverty is indi-
` cated

Note : (11 A simple mathematical model is suggested
where in planets have the following numerical values : Sun
(1) Moon (I or 3 depending on its pakshabala i.e. from
sukla ekadasi to krusna panchami 3 points) ; Mars (1) ;
Mercury (1); Jupiter (3); Venus (2); Saturn (2) ; Rahu (3);
Ketu (2). Add the numerical values of the benefics in 2nd,
` 4th, Sth, 8th & 9th houses and malefics in 3rd & 6th and
substract the values of the benefics in 3rd & 6th and

---

## Page 99

Chapter I Quarter ला 89

malefics ` in 2nd, 4th, 5th, 8th & 9th houses. The nett
balance, if positive, indicates wealth & prosperity, and if
negative, it indicates losses and poverty. This exercise
~ should be carried out from the Arudha lagna, the seventh
house, Paka Arudha lagna and Paka Arudha Saptama.

(ii) Similarly, financial downturns can be predicted
during the period of benefits in 3rd & 6th and malefics in
2nd, 4th,5th,8th & 9th houses from the Arudha lagna.

1.3.35. मातरि गुरौ शक्रे चन्द्रे वा राजकीयाः॥

If Jupiter, Venus or the Moon are present in the fifth
house (from Arudha lagna or its seventh house or Paka
Arudha lagna or Paka Arudha Saptama) political / govern-
mental authority is obtained or the native becomes a Govt.
emissary.

Note : (i) The fifth house deals with authority from
the king. If a benefic is present, the person is appointed by
Government/ king. The point is that benefics cause
elevation and indicate the begining/sustenance of the
Rajyogas.

(it) Mata = 65/12=5 Rem.

1.3.36. कर्मणि दासे वा पापे सेनान्यः॥
If malefics are in the 3rd & 6th houses instead, the
native joins the armed forces.

Note : (i) The pairs are based on argala and
virodhargala i.e. intervention and obstruction. If the inter-
vention (argala) and its obstruction (virodhargala) are of
equal strength, the results are neither success nor failure
and seizure results i.e. stalemate If both planets are malefies,
~ ~ this shows imprisonment while benefits cause house arrest
etc. ` `

(ii) Pascha = 61/12 = 1 Rem ; implies lagna and could

is from lagna, the person is physically imprisoned or
physically obstructed; if from Arudha lagna his rise and
image suffer a setback while from atmakarak , bondage of
the soul results and spiritual growth is obstructed/stunted.

(ui) Ripu = 12 ; Bhagya = 2; Konas are 5th & 9th ;

& 6th instead of ‘8th & 6th’.

1.3.42. शुक्राद गौण पदस्थो UE: सूर्य दुष्टो नेत्र हा॥
Venus and Gaunapada aspected or conjoined by Rahu
& the Sun causes blindness.

Note : (i) This is a difficult stanza. ‘Sukra’ could also
mean lagna (sukra = 25/12 = 1 Rem ) and '‘Gauna ' could
also mean the fifth (Gauna = 53 /12 = 5 Rem ) . Thus,
Gauna pada has been interpreted by some astrologers as
the Mantrarodha or the arudha of the 5th house, while
others interpret this as the fifth house from Arudha lagna.
Popularly Gauna pada means upapada or the arudha of the
twelfth house.

(11) Jaimini has used the names of planets and ‘sukra’
implies ‘Venus’ as ‘Gaunapada’ refers to ‘upapada’. There
are two conditions gives in the stanza : (a) venus should bg
conjoined or aspected by Rahu (this indicates eye disease
also) and (b) upapada should be conjoined or aspected by
the sun (this indicates very weak eyesight). If both condi-
tions (a) & (b) merge, blindness is sure to occur. Readers

may refer to a few examples at the end of this Quarter.

first or fourth house. This may occur from lagna, Arudha
lagna or Atmakarak.

14.1. उपपदं पदं पित्रनुचरात्‌॥ |
The arudha of the 12th house (counted Zodiacally) is
the upapada. : .

Note : (i) The upapada is also called the Gauna pada.
Take thel2th house from lagna reckoned zodiacally. Deter-
mine the arudha pada of the sign. This is the upapada.

(ii) Scholars hold divergeant views on the reckonin g of
the sign in the twelfth saying that the count ‘should ~
be rerverse for samapada signs ascending while others prefer

reverse count for even signs. These views are incorrect.

142. तत्र पापस्य पापयोगे प्रव्रज्या दारनाशो वा॥

If the second from upapada has malefic aspects or
conjunctions the native loses his wife or renounces the
world. |

Note : (i) (Tatra =26 /12=2 Rem). The upapada, (the
arudha of the 12th house) is different from darapada (the
arudha of the 7th house.) It deals with the institution of
marriage and children, while the darapada deals with the
sexual appetite and the business/finances in the chart. This
differentiation is of vital importance in making predictions
as, it is possible that young people may come together and
still remain unmarried. There are also many people who
have affairs outside marriage. ,

---

## Page 118

108 . Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

(ii) In the modern context, the darapada should also
be examined before predicting renunciation priesthood
(pravrajya yoga as there are many who remain Bachelors
“and are still in the social stream. Jupiter is the karaka for
upapada as Venus is the karak for darapada.

The Sun is not a malefic for matters concerning the
upapada.

sun is never adverse towards the upapada.

‘of spouse occurs.

Moving reverse in manduka gati from the ninth the

Note : Umpteen interpretations have been given for
this but of no avail Nilakantha interprets ‘adesha’ to
mean upapada and its lord However it means that the third
from the sign arrived at by counting (as per ‘kramat’)
Again panchmamsa (= 657/12 = 9 Rem) indicates that: for
an even sign ascending the 9th house lord indicates the
first pregnancy while for a male sign ascending the fifth
house lord indicates the first pregnancy. ‘Kramat in the
` present context means Manduka gati or the frog jump.
“Thus if the first preguancy is from the 9th house, the
subsequent children will be from the lords of the 7th, 5th,
31d 1st etc. respectively (the frog jump is to the third sign).
Instead, if the first Pregnancy is from the 5th house, the
subsequent children with be judged from the lords of the
7th, 9th, 11th, etc.

The male planets are the Sun Rahu, Jupiter and Mars

“while the female planets are Venus, Moon, & Ketu. The
eunuch planets are Mercury and Saturn. If the Lord of the
child joins a male planets or a planet in exaltation the child
will be a male . If the lord of the child joins a female
planet or a planet is debility the child will be a female. If
male signs disposits the lord, a male issue is indicated
‘while if a female sign disposits the lord a female issue is
indicated.

Since the fifth and the ninth houses indicate children

EXPLANATORY NOTES :

In this quarter sage Jaimini focuses on the immediate .
, family of the native comprising of the spouse and children
‘and subsequently on the brothers / sisters of spouse and
self. In the previous quarter the sage had .explained the
concept of Darapada (Arudha of seventh house) whereby
` the financial status and physical relationship with spouse
(and other women) were explained. The focus now comes
“on the spouse for whom the upapada (Arudha of twelfth
house) is reserved. The upapada also indicates the procre-
ative abilities of the native. However, the sage stresses the
importance of an indepth microscopic examination of this
latter aspect from the saptamsa (D-7 chart) as it is likely
that many births may occur within a timespan of two
hours (approximate period of rising of an ascendant) and a
‘more detailed study is required for such a sensitive subject.
For the convenience of readers Table 1.22 provides
the saptamsas. Subsequently, the sage explains the prin-
ciples to predict the presence (or otherwise) of co=borns of
spouse from the upapada. This principle is also applicable
for the co-borns of the native from Arudha Lagna. How-
ever, for a more detailed examination the Navamsa (D9)
chart should be used for all matters concerning spouse and
the Drekkana (D3) should be use for ones own co-borns.

CASE STUDIES: UPAPADA

Chart 21: Male born on 1st of January 1953 at 5:09 am
IST at 31701, 75E48, INDIA. Atmakarak : Mercury;
Darakarak: Venus; upapada (UL): Gemini; AL : Arudha
Lagna. | ः ः

MALE IST JAK. 1953
5:09 AM IST 31 NOI

75 E 48 INDIA

## Page 130

120 Jamini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

In Chart 21. Scorpio rises with the atmakarak Mer-
cury in it indicating the potential for a Rajyoga. However,
Mercury is debilitated in the navamsa indicating Rajbhanga
Neecha yoga. The native although born in a well-to-do
family has wasted away his years in pleasures, and does
not follow any occupation. His half hearted attempts at
business have been disastrous during the last seventeen
years (upto 1996), thereby proving the vital importance of
the Atmakarak in making or marring a chart.

The upapada is in the eighth house in Gemini and
Mercury, its lord, is already involved in a debilitating
yoga. The native is still not married. The moon in the
eighth house (that too as the lord of badhak-obstactes has
added to the damage as the chandrastama dosha comes on
_ the upapada. The'way out of this quagmire is seen from the
second from upapada (cancer). Ketu the mokshkarak (spiri-
tual guide for emancipation) is placed in cancer and indi-
cates Brahmacharya (celebacy). The second house lord
is the Moon and as explained earlier, is the badhakesh
(chief obstructor of the chart) having chandrastama
dosha is placed in its exalted and fixed navamsa Taurus
indicating unsurmountable and very high order of obstales.
No doubt that the native is still a bachelor and
inspite of his best attempts, has failed to find a suitable
companion

Compare this horoscope to chart-13 of Shri A.B
Vajpagee who is also a bachelor. Venus, the seventh lord
of Rasi chart (in both charts) is in the twelfth house 10 the
navamsa with Saturn. However, the Atmakarak Mercury 15
very strong in the chart of Shn Vajpayee.

"give a very powerful Rajyoga (through spouse as it is lord

INFERENCE :

“ff Stanzas 1.1.25 to 1.1.27 which pertain to method of
counting and others should be understood as follows :-

(a) That for matter concerning the native the reckoning of
houses from Arudha lagna is always zodiacal.

(b) That for matter concerning the spouse the reckoning
of houses from the upapada is always zodiacal.

(©) That for matter concerning co-borns of the native the
elder from the eleventh and youngers from the third,
the reckoning from the Arudha lagna is zodiacal or `
reverse order depending on whether the sign is odd or
even (and not oddfooted/evenfooted)..

Chapter I Quarter IV . 139

That for matters concerning co-boms of the spouse
the houses are reckoned from the upapada in zodiacal
or reverse order depending on whether the upapada
sign is odd or even.

That for matters concerning co-born from the Drekkana -
(D-3) this zodiacal/ reverse count would depend on
whether the ascendant is odd or even. The first elder/
younger sibling is seen from the eleventh/third house
respectively and the subsequent are seen by moving in
Manduka Gati (frog jump --3 signs; after covering six
signs it crawls to the next and again starts jumping to

। every third house).

That the lords of the respective houses unless con-
joined by other planets determine the sex of the
sibling. If they are placed in odd signs (except Gemini
& Aquarius) or in Pisces or Cancer the sex is male.

If they are placed in even signs (except Pisces &

Cancer) or in Gemini or Aquarius the sex is female. If

“exalted the sex is male and if debilitated the sex is |
‘female. If conjoined by other planets, the strongest

amongst these shall determine the sex. The Sun, Jupi-
ter, Rahu & Mars are males. The Moon , Venus, &
Ketu are females and Mercury & Saturn are neuters or
may show a female/male respectively.

That for matters concerning children from the saptamsa
chart (D-7) the zodiacal/reverse count would depand
on the nature of the ascending sign as being odd/even
respectively. The first-child is seen from the fifth
houses and subsequent children are seen from every

third therefrom (ie. 7th, 9th, 11th etc.) as per manduka

gati.

Normally the nodes (Rahu & Ketu) tend to limit the
number of issues.

Chapter II Quarter I

2.1.1. आयुः पितृ दिनेशाश्याम्‌॥।

Longevity 15 estimated from the lords of lagna and the
. eighth house

Note : (1) Pitru=6/12=1 Rem ; Dina = 8 Rem,. In this
work Jaimini has outlined the two most appropriate methods
for estimating the longevity. The first method uses three pairs
of signs of which the first pair is that occupied by the lord of
the ascendant and the eighth house.

0) There are two schools of thought in determining
the eighth house for use in the Ayur stanzas. The first
counts the eighth house zodiacally from the ascendant and
the other uses table 2.1.

2.1.2. प्रथमयोरुत्तरयोर्वा दीर्घम॥।

If the lords of the first and eighth are both in movable
signs or if one is in a fixed sign and the other is in a dual
sign, long life is indicated.

2.1.3. प्रथमद्वितीययोरन्तयोर्वा मधयम्‌॥

If the lords of the first and eighth are both in dual
signs or if one is in a fixed sign and the and the other in a
movable sign a middle life span is indicated.

* For these signs the eighth house from the lord of the

---

## Page 152

142 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras -

|
: Eighth House

“sign would have to be taken as the lord of the ascendant and
eighth house are one and the same. If however, the eighth
and ascendant lords are still the same the eighth from these

“signs will replace them. For example if Mars is in Aries in
the ascendant, the eighth house is Scorpio and its lord will be `
Mars. Hence, the eighth from Scorpio i.e. Sagittarius should
be considered and its lord Jupiter becomes 8th lord.

2.1.4, मधययोराद्यन्तयो्वां हीनम्‌॥

If the lords of the first and eighth are both in fixed
signs or if one is in a dual sign and the other i¥ a movable
sign, a short life span is indicated.

Note : (1) The principle employed is that if both are
in signs of identical nature (i.e. fixed, dual or movable)
then the same prevails. If however, the two signs are of
different natpre by the principle of exclusion the nature not
covered indicates longivity. Thus, if the two signs are fixed

---

## Page 153

Chapter II Quarter I ` 143

and movable, the nature not covered viz dual, indicates the
longevity. Brahma, Visnu and Rudra the three aspects of
God as the creater, sustainer and destroyer are the presid-
ing deities of movable, dual and fixed signs respectively.
Thus, the movable nature indicative of long life, dual
nature of middle life span and fixed nature of short life
span. The standard life span for this purpose (for human
charts) is 108 years wherein the short life compartment is
0-36 years, middle life compartment 36 - 72 years and long
life compartment 72 - 108 years. For other animals or
“temporary bodies like elected parliaments, the total life
span can be divided into three parts.

2.1.5. एवं मन्दचन्द्राभ्याम्‌॥

These rules (given in the preceding stanzas 2.1.2 to =
214) are to be 20180 to the signs occupied by the Moon
and Saturn.

Note :- The signs occupied by Moon and Saturn form
the second pair and the life compartment should be
determined from them. Most commentators including
Neelakantha etc. al. have taken 'Manda' to mean the
ascendant (Manda = 85 / 12 = 1 Rem) implying that the
ascendant and moon signs are the second pair. However
my translation is supported by parrasara.

Parasara :- “* अथाऽन्यदपि वक्षयामि श्रृणु त्वं द्विजसत्तम।

लगनहोराविलग्नाभ्यां ततीयं परिचिन्तयेत्‌।'*

third pair.

2.1.7. संवादात्‌ प्रामाण्यम्‌॥।
If two of the three pairs indicate identical spans, the
particular longivity is to be declared.

Note : (i) We have three pairs of lagna & eighth
lords, Saturn & Moon and lagna & Hora lagna indicating
longivity compartments vide stanzas 2.1.2 to 2.1.4. If two
of these show a particular span, this will prevail.

(i) Parasara gives additional hints.

“dt योगत्रयेणैव नखचन्द्रसमान्दकाः।
योगद्वयेन वस्वाशा योगैकेन रसांकका॥
मधये योगत्रयेणैव खाष्टतुल्याब्दकाः स्मृता।
TAM योगडये नाडन्रयोगैकेनान्धिाषणिमताः।

- योगद्वयेन षटत्रिंशत्‌ यौगैकंन च खाब्धाय॥

Thus, if two pairs show full life span it is upto-108

years, if two pairs show middle life span it is upto 72 years

and if two pairs show short life span it is upto 36 years.
What happens to this if the third pair is different or the
same 15 given in table 2.2.

Thus, for example, if all three pairs show short life the
primary life span is 32 years.

2.1.8. विसंवादे पितृकालतः॥

If the life span indicated by all the three pairs are
different, that indicated by the hora lagna (and lagna pair)
will prevail.

Note : However, this will cause suitable adjustment in
the maximum life span. For example, if all the three pairs
indicate short, middle & long life and the pair of Hora |
lagna and lagna indicate long life, the lowest rung in table
2.2 for a combination of Long life + long life + short life
= 96 years will have to be reduced by 8 years (88 years
mar) to suit the combination of Long life + middle life +
~ short life . In this manner the stanzas should be under-

stood.

© 2.1.9. पितृलाभे चन््रमन्दाभ्याम्‌॥

If, however, the Moon is in ‘the ascendant or the
seventh house, the longevity indicated by the moon and
Saturn pair shall prevail.

Note :- (1) Pitru = 1 , Labha = 7. Stanzas 2.1.8 &
2.1.9 are riders applicable only when the life span indi-
cated by all the: three pairs are different. Parasara has a
similar view.

(1) Parasara gives additional hints on fixing the
longivity.
“qui राश्यादिगे चान्ते हानिर्मधयेडनुपाततः।

Note : (i) The navamsa dasas are Ayur dasas and have

(ii) The dasa sign itself is the Dwara (door) and the
Bahya is the sign obtained by counting as many signs from
Dwara as it has gained from the lagna. Thus, if Ares
‘ascends and the dasa is of the fourth sign Cancer, the
Dwara is Cancer and the Bahya is Libra (four signs from
Cancer.

(iii) The 'Dwara' and ‘Bahya’ are different from Paka’
and ‘Bhoga’. The sign occupied by the lord of the dasa rasi
is the Paka and the Arudha of the dasa rasi is the Bhoga
(fruit). Thus, in the above example if the Moon is in
Saggitarius, the Paka rasi is Saggitarius and the Arudha
Pada of Cancer, the sixth from Saggitarius i.e. Taurus is
the Bhoga Rasi. (See Fig 2.3) Symbolically the Dwara
Rasi is the doorway through which the soul is to leave the

2.1.20. योगात्समे स्वस्मिन्‌ विपरीतम्‌॥

If the Atmakarak is in the seventh or ninth house from
lagna the life span indicated is reversed.

Note : 'Yoga Vipareetam' implies a Vipareeta Ayur
Yoga in the lines of a Vipareeta Raj yoga. Thus if the
longivity arrived at (by the methods given earlier is long
life, it is reduced to middle life and middle to ‘short life
wife short life becomes long life. Vipareeta Ayur Yoga
means change of longivity simultaneously affecting the
longivity of a relative indicated by the atmakarak. Thus,

“Yor example, if short life is indicated initially and the
“atmakarak sun is in the ninth house, the natives longivity is
increased but his father (Sun) passes away early.

2.1.22. रोगेशयोस्ततः एेक्ये योगे वा मधयम्‌॥

` gives long life. This is to be understood from ‘yoga

vipareetam

(it) The following is traditionally taught

(a) Determine the stronger amongst the first and sev-

eighth from the stronger sign is always reckoned directly.
If the 8th lord is placed in a kendra (quadrant) from lagna,
purna ayus (72 - 108 years) is indicated . If the 8th lord is
in a Panapara (Succeedent), madhya ayus (36 - 72 years) is
indicated and if, in an apoklimas, alpa ayus (0 - 36 years)
is obtained.

(b) JAGANNATHS RULE : Divide the Ayur Khanda
(longivity portion) into four parts of 9 years each . If the
8th lord is in the 10th, 11th or 12th from lagna’ the death
is in the first part. If the 8th lord is in the 7th, 8th or 9th
death is in the 2nd half. If the 8th lord is in the 4th, 5th or
6th, death is in the 3rd part and if in the Ist, 2nd or 3rd
death is predicted in the last part.

80. vipareeta ayus yoga is to be predicted due to the -

Note : Malefics in the 2nd and 12th from a sign cause
papakartari yoga and also indicate Bandhana yoga while
malefics in both Sth and 9th indicate bandhana yoga. Such

a placement of malefics causes Kakshya hrasa or reduction - -

in longivity. Reduction occurs from Purna (108) to Madhya
(72), Alpa (36), Yogarishta (20) or Balarishta (8) in that
order. Malefics in Ist & 7th cause disease resulting in
reduction in longivity Saturn & Mars / Ketu so placed
cause Unmada yoga (madness / epilepsy)

2.1.46, स्वभावेशो महेश्वरः॥

The lord of the 8th house from the Atmakaraka is
called Maheswara

Note : If maybe noted that there are 12 signs in the
zodiac and, as per stanza 2.1.35 each will have an eighth
house termed Rudra Rasi. All such signs excepting the
sign occupied by Jupiter are called Rudra Rasis thereby
giving eleven Rudras (Ekadas Rudra). Now, the lord of the
8th house from the sign occupied by atmakaraka gets a
higher status than the other Rudras and is called Maheswara.
The Bhagwat (Gita also indicates this difference when Sri
Krishna says" amongst the Rudras I am Shankara (or
Maheswara)”. The philosophical difference is that each of
` the other Rudras simply destroys the body whereas
Maheswara emancipates the soul (atma).

2.1.47. स्वोच्ये स्वभे रिपुभावेश प्राणि॥

If the 8th lord from Atmakaraka is exalted or in own
sign, the lord of the 8th / 12th from -it, whichever is
stronger, becomes Maheswara.

Note : (i) Ripu = 12 Bhava = 44 / 12 = 8 Rem. This
15 the first rider to determination of Maheswara vide stanza
2.1.46 and is based on the principle that the 8th lord in
exaltation or in own sign loses its sting to kill and del-
egates the power to another i.e. the lord of the 8th / 12th
from the sign where it is placed

(11) It is possible to interpret 'Ucche’ as 12th and ‘Bhe
as 4th implying that if the 8th lords in the 12th / 4th from
the atmakarak, the rider is activated. However, this does

---

## Page 168

158 ` Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

not justify the disqualification of the 8th lord as
Maheswara .

(iii) It is also possible to interpret ‘Ripu bhavesha' as
8th / 12th lord from the Atmakarak on the grounds of
implication. But then, the stanza should have read as
“Ucche Bhave Swaripu bhavesha Prani”.

2.1.48. 'पाताभ्यां योगे स्वस्य तयोर्वा रोगे ततः॥ |

If Rahu or Ketu become Maheswara of, if Rahu or
Ketu is in the 1st / 8th from Atmakaraka, the sixth planet
or sixth lord respectively becomes Maheswara

Note : (i) (5४ = 1; Roga = 32 ८ 12 = 8 Rem)
‘Patabhyam yoga’ has been interpreted in the same lines as
'Rahu, Yoge' in a later stanza 2.1.52 and 'Tatah’ has been
interpreted in the same lines as in stanza 2.1.50 wherein
Tatah = 66 / 12 = 6 Rem

(ii) The second rider to determination of Maheswara
is that if Rahu or Ketu become Maheswara, the sixth planet
from them .in the order of the weekdays becomes
Maheswara. Thus, Mercury shall replace Rahu and Jupiter
shall replace Ketu as Maheswara.

(iii) The third rider to Maheswara determination is
that if Rahu / Ketu is with the atmakarak or the 8th sign
from it, the lord of the sixth sign instead shall become
Maheswara (because the sixth house is the 8th counted in |
the reverse direction from Atmakarak due to Rahu &
Ketu)

Additional Notes : (2) With the Atmakarak in Aries,
Ketu as the co - lord of Scorpio could qualify for Maheswara
and if the AK is in Cancer, Rahu as the co - lord of
Aquarius may qualify for Maheswara. Also if exalted Ve-
nus or strong Jupiter as temporary Maheswara is in Pisces,

Rahu as the 12th lord competes for becoming Maheswara.
Similarly with strong Moon or exalted Jupiter in Cancer as
temporary Maheswara. Rahu would come into the compe-

` .. coming Maheswara if exalted Sun or strong Mars is in

Aries as temporary Maheswara or if exalted Ketu or strong
Jupiter is in Saggitarius as temporary Maheswara.

(b) In the third rider, Rahu could himself become the
atmakarak or either of the nodes could join the atmakarak
or be in the 8th house from it. Then the 8th lord from
atmakarak shall become Maheswara. Basically we are count-

due to the influence of the nodes to arrive at the 6th house
.whose lord becomes Maheswara

(c) An intelligent question would be as to what hap-
pens if this sixth lord (8th lord in reverse reckoning) in
exalted or placed in own sign? Then the stronger of the
lords of the 8th/12th from it becomes Maheswara. Now,
what happens if such a 8th/12th lord is Rahu/Ketu? Then
Mercury/Jupiter replaces Rahu/Ketu respectively as
Maheswara

disqualified. If lagna is stronger, the 7th to 12th houses

the signs in the Ist to 6th hpuse constitute the invisible '. -

half’

Step 4 : From amongst the qualifying lords, the stron-
` gest becomes Brahma.

(if) What happens if none qualify? Then the weaker of
the lagna/seventh should be considered for locating Brahma.

What happens if none qualify even now? Then the last -
condition of location in the visible half should be ignored
if a lord is in an odd sign in the invisible half. If all planets
are in even signs, then the condition of location in an odd
sign should be dropped. In this manner the intelligent
, astrologer should identify Brahma

` 2.1.50. ब्रह्मणि शनौ पातयो्वां ततः॥

If Saturn, Rahu or Ketu become Brahma, then the
sixth planet (reckoned in the order of weekdays) becomes
Brahma. *

Note : (1) Rahu and Ketu are reckoned as the eighth &
ninth planets after the seven from sun to saturn. If Saturn
becomes Brahma, then Mars the 6th from it replaces it as

Brahma. Similarly, Mercury replaces Rahu and Jupiter
` replaces ketu as Brahma. (Tatah=66/12=6 Rem.) `

(ii) Parasana has a similar view.

2.1.51. बहूनां योगे स्वजातीयः॥

If more than one planet qualifies for Brahma, the one
with a higher longitude (in the sign) becomes Brahma.
2.1.52. राहुयोगे विपरीतम्‌

. sign. वि । ।

2.1.53, ब्रह्मा स्वभावेशो भावस्थः॥

If the lord of the eighth from atmakarak is in the eighth
itself, it qualifies as Brahma.

Note: If the lord of the 8th from atmakarak is in other
signs, if becomes Maheswara (vide stanza 2.1.46), but in
the 8th itself it cannot be Maheswara (stanza 2.1.47) and
becomes Brahma _

2.1.54. विवादे बली॥ ,.

If two or more planets claim to be Brahma, the
strongest should be taken

situation rarely arises where among the contending planets

stanza 2.1.51

2.1.56. तत्रपि महेश्वर भावेश त्रिकोणाब्दे॥

During the Brahma dasa of the sign having Maheswara
the antardasa will be of a sign in trines to the sign occu-
pied by the eighth lord from Maheswara.

Note : 'Tatrapi’ refers to the preceding stanza wherein
death takes place during Brahma dasa of Maheswara, The
sign occupied by the lord of the eighth house from
Maheswara or its trines furnishes the death inflicting
antardasa.

2.1.57. स्व कर्म चित्त रिप रोग नाथ प्राणि मारकः।

` (killer)

atmakarak is used in Brahma dasas

Note : (Kala=31/12=7), If is a well known astrologi-

the same and these become superfluous if the interpretation.
of Neelakantha is to be accepted. It is unlikely that Yaimini
would be superfluous and the interpretation given is based

on sound astrological protenical principles.

. Explanatory Notes :

At the outset I caution the readers that there is no fool
proof method for determining longivity. Most standard
texts refer to Amsayur, Astakavargayu, Nisargikayu and
Pindaya. However these mathematical models are, at most
‘times, quite off the mark. Finally both Parasara (BPHS
. Chapter 45) and Jaimini (Chapter 2 & 3) have explained
three important systems. These are (a) the three pairs of
determinants (b) the eighth lord in quadrants etc. and (c)
the strength of lords of the first, tenth, eighth and fifth
houses. However, infantile longevity should also be con-
firmed from the Pataki chakra and other astrological tools.
While the third method is dealt with in a subsequent
chapter, some additional clues have been indicated in the
case studies. oc

2. The method of Kakshya Vriddhi and Kakshya Hrasa
. (i.e. increase/decrease of longivity compartment) is no mean
task. While most astrologers are able to explain its use in

---

## Page 174

164

Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

historical cases, they fail in predictions. The rules are as
follows:

(a)

0)

©

®

2)

Decrease in longivity compartment occurs if Saturn
conjoins/aspects the planets contributing to the

‘longivity determination. However this will not happen

if Saturn in one of the planets itself. For example if
Saturn and the moon determine the longivity, an auto-
matic reduction does not occur just because Saturn is

involved. If Saturn is in its own sign or its exaltation

this reduction will not occur. Instead, if afflicted,
Saturn will tend to adversely affect the longivity.

Increase in longivity compartment is caused by the
strong position of unaffilicted Jupiter in the ascendant
or the seventh house

Instead if the ascendant/seventh is subjected to

papakartari yoga or has malefics in trines (1,5,9)

‘kakshya hrasa occurs, Benefics in trines or subhakartari

yoga causes kakshya vriddhi. Similar estimation should
be done from the atmakarak

The ascendant lord in a malefic sign or debilitated or
afflicted by malifics causes Rasi hrasa while in a

_ beneficial sign or with benefics or in exaltation, Rasi

vriddhi occurs. Similarly estimate from Jupiter

| (Thus, atmakarak is the karaka for lagna as Jupiter is

the karak for paka lagna)

If a strong Moon or Venus joins/aspects the lagna/
paka lagna rasi vriddhi occurs.

It will not be correct to attempt any mathematical

model and experience is the best teacher.

Pravrajya Yoga : The Aroodha lagna in Leo has
malefics Saturn in 2nd, Rahu in 4th, Sun in 5th and Mars
in 9th houses and benefics Jupiter in 3rd, Mercury &
Venus in 6th and Ketu (Benefic) in 6th from Atmakarak all
contributing to the pravrajya yoga leading to renunciation
of worldly life (stanza 1.3.30 to 36). It maybe noted that
benefics in 3rd & 6th from arudha lagna cause poverty but,
they did not make him a coward or one lacking in valour
in any way. The Arudha lagna is the "Image" that one has
in this materialistic world and since all planets excepting
the moon (mind) are contributing to the pravrajya yoga he
became a sanyasi. The upapada (Leo) has the same situa-
tion and inspite of his agreeing to marry (moon is a benefic
in the second house) his spiritual guide (Bhratrukaraka
Saturn) was able to prevent it. In the battle between the
moon (family) and Saturn (teacher) the moon has a higher
longitude and should have won but for the presence of
atmakarak Sun a

Planets in mutual kendras become paraspara karakas
and in the scheme, the Sun had the option of supporting
either the Moon or Saturn and since it is in the fifth from
Arudha lagna contributing to the pravrajra yoga, it sup-
ported Saturn in the last moment. His father died one day
before the wedding. The rest is history.

weigh in favour of cancer being the maraka Navamsa dasa.

Note : Malefic aspects on the weaker one make it
very weak and evil while benefics aspecting the stronger
give it the strength to kill. The point is that a complete
evaluation of the relative strength on the basis of exalta-
tion, beneficial aspect etc. for the stronger significator and
debilitation, malefic aspect etc. of the weaker significator
“will have to be made before declaring results. If the weaker
significator kills, the attitude is one of vengence / anger on
the concerned person while if the stronger is the death
inflictor the attitude is one of providing relief from suffer-

ng.

Explanato ry Notes

In this quarter the sage has briefly explained the
principles underlying the cause of death and the methodol-
ogy of timing the death of near and dear ones. The Sun or
Venus (semen) shall indicate father whereas the Moon or
Mars (blood) shall indicate the mother. In a similar way
the fixed significators (not temporal nor natural significators)
are used to ascertain the longivity of other relatives. For
example, the Darapada (Arudha of seventh house) and
Venus (natural significator for spouse) are examined to
determine the direction of her residence before marriage

conjugal harmony etc whereas the upapada (Arudha of ..

twelfth house) and Jupiter (fixed significator for spouse)
are examined to determine the fruits of marriage, length of `
married life (i.e. death of spouse) etc. The other fixed
significators have been explained in Chapter I, Quarter ~ 1
These subtle differences should be borne in mind while
examining the horoscopes

The third house from Arudha lagna can be examined
for determining the cause of death of the native while. the -
sign in the third will indicate the place of death. While the
shoola dasas have been explained in subsequent chapters,
these have been used in the case studies. However, the
findings in Rasi chart should also be confirmed from the
vargas (divisional charts).

DEATH OF FATHER :

~The Sun with the conjunction of the Moon (exalted) is
stronger than Venus. Thus the Sun is qualified as the fixed
, significator of father. The third house from the Sun is
- Cancer a beneficial sign indicating home. Jupiter (exalted
is in Cancer showing a peaceful death more so since it is
aspected by the exalted Moon and the Sun. Jupiter in the
third would indicate prior knowledge of some kind either
10 the self or close associates. The natives father went into
a coma and passed away after 7 days at home. Since
~ Jupiter in the third house is aspected by the moon, stanza
2.2.22 should also apply and the father was unable to
consume food when in coma and had to given the drip.

The eighth signs from Taurus and Scorpio are Gemini
and Saggitarius respectively (Table 2.1) and Mercury with
the conjunction of two malefics is qualified as the Rudra

+ planet for father. Thus, death can occur during the shoola
dasas of the earthy signs (stanza 2.2.24 Sun in Taurus) or `
during the shoola dasas of the Airy signs (stanza 2.2.6
Mercury in Gemini). The shoola dasas for father begin

from Libra (as the 9th house with exalted Saturn aspected

signs aspected by it. Thus, Libra, Capricorn & Taurus are
eliminated. The dasas of Virgo and Gemini would come
very late thereby indicating demise of father in Aquarius
Pitru shoola dasa. The father passed away in 42nd year in
the fifth shoola dasa (Aquarius).

Brahma.

the next Ayur dasa mentioned by the stage. The dasa
begins from the sign occupied by Brahma. The movable
fixed and dual signs alternatively contribute 7,8&9 years
respectively

(हो) The param ayus (maximum Longivity) “under this
dasa is 96 years.

2.3.5. अथ प्राण;
The sources of strength are being enunciated.

Note: There are different methods for calculating the
strength of signs and planets. Most standard text have very
cumbersome mathematical models for this purpose. How-
ever, Jaimini has simplified the calculation such that in a
glance, the relative. strength between two signs can easily
be judged. The sage teaches four sources of strength for
signs. Unless otherwise specified, these are to be used in
the order of the following stanza 2.3.6 to 2.3.17. Some -
mathematical models have been attempted, but it will be
noted that the source”of strength is based on the principles
of exclusion. For example if two signs are being compared
the mathematical model assumes that all the stanzas 2.3.6

---

## Page 208

198 . Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

to 2.3.17 are applicable. However this is not so. If one sign
has the conjunction of the Atmakarak planet, it will prove
“to be stronger than all other signs in the chart and if all the
planets are in the other sign, the mathematical model
shows the latter to be stronger thereby giving erroneous
results. It is suggested that these rules be applied to a few
charts and two signs compared to develop expertise.

2.3.6, कारकयोगः प्रथमोभानाम्‌॥
The first source of strength is the presence of the
Atmakarak planet in the sign

2.3.7. साम्ये भूयसा॥

In case both the signs are not occupied by the
Atmakarak, the conjunction of a large number of planets
. will show the stronger sign

2.3.8, ततस्तुड्‌गादिः॥
7 both the signs have equal number of planets, then
. the status of the planets like exaltation/ own sign etc. will
render one sign stronger.

` 2.3.9. निसर्गेतस्ततः॥

If both signs are still equally strong, then the natural
order of strength (i.e. a dual sign is stronger than a fixed
sign and a movable sign is the weakest ) shall prevail.

Note: Some authors give the natural strength of the
planets under this stanza. However this is out of context as
the strength of two signs are being compared and the
natural strength of signs with dual signs being the stron-
gest, fixed signs relatively weaker and movable signs the
` weakest is referred to.

2.3.10. तदभावे स्वामिनः इत्यंभावः॥
If both signs are unoccupied, then the sign whose
Lord becomes the Atmakarak is stronger -

---

## Page 209

Chapter II Quarter III ` 199

Note: Having failed to select the stronger from among
the signs, the Lord of the signs is used for sources of
strength. If either of the signs has the Atmakarak as its
Lord, it is stronger. However, if both or none have
atmakarak as its lord, the next stanza is used.

2.3.11. आग्रायतोऽत्र विशेषात्‌॥

। In case none of the signs have the atmakarak as its
Lord then the sign whose Lord has advanced more in

degrees (irrespective of signs) is stronger.

2.3.12. प्रातिवेशिकः पुरुषे॥

। If the two signs have the same Lord of if their Lords
have equal longitude, then odd signs are strong if thew
Lord is in an even sign and even signs gain strength if their
Lord is in an odd sign.

2.3.13. इति प्रथमः॥
Thus ends the first source of strength.

2.3.14. स्वामि गुरुज्ञदूग्योगो द्वितीयः॥
The second source of strength of sign is the aspect or
conjunction of its Lord, the atmakarak, Jupiter or Mercury.

Note : It is possible that in some instances like the
chara dasas, padakrama dasas or Navamsa dasas the sec-
ond source of strength is exclusively used instead of falling
in order after the first. The sources of strength are exclu-
sive of each other and only in case where one fails 10
identify one sign as the stronger, is the other used .

2.3.15. स्वामिनस्तृतीयः॥
The third source of strength comes from the place-
ment of the Lord of a sign.

2.3.16. स्वात्स्वामिनः कण्टकादिष्वपारदौर्बल्यम्‌॥
If the Lord of a sign is in quadrants, succeedent or

---

## Page 210

200 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

` precedant sign from the atmakarka - the strength will be
proportionately declining,

Note: (i) Thus if the Lord of a sign is in a kendra
(Quadrant) from the atmakraka it is stronger than any other
sign whose Lord is in a parapara (Succeedant). The, sign
whose lord is in an Apoklimas (precedant) from the
atmakaraka, is the weakest . :

(1) This source of strength is used in Lagna Kendradi
Graha/Rashi dasas, Atmakaraka Kendradi Graha/Rashi dasas
etc.

2.3.17. चतुर्थतः पुरुषे॥
The fourth source of strength of sign is the conjunc-
 tion/aspect of malefics (or a malefic ownership).

Note: The aspect \conjunction of malefics or the sign
being owned by a malefics makes it stronger than other to
inflict death. This source of strength is exclusively used in
Ayur dasas (Longivity calculation ) of the self and others.

2.3.18. पितृ लाभ प्रथम प्राण्यादि शूलदशा नियणि॥
The stronger amongst the ascendant and seventh house
"is used to reckon the Shoola dasas.

Note: (Pitru =61/12=1. Labha = 43/12 = 7). The
Shoola dasas are reckoned from the ascendant or the
seventh whichever is stronger. These dasas are always
zodiacal. For humah charts, these are for 9 years each,

2.3.19. पितु-लाभ-पुत्रः प्राण्यादिःपितुः |
| The stronger amongst the ninth and third houses ini-
tiates the shoola dasa for father.

Note: (Pitru =21/12=9), 'Adi’ refers to the 1st and 7th
` signs from the 9th house i.e. the 9th and 3rd houses. It is
a well known astrological principle that the 9th house
` represents the father.
