## Page 211

Chapter II Quarter I 201

2.3.20. आदर्शादि्मांतुः॥
The stronger amongst the fourth and tenth houses
initiates the Shoola dasa for mother

Note: ‘Adarsha = 580/12=4', ‘Adi’ means the 1st/7th
from the 4th 1.6. the 4th or 10th houses. It is a well known
astrological principle that the 4th house represents mother.
Neelakantha's interpretation of Adarsha as Abhimukha is
not acceptable and is completely out of context in the
present stanza.

2.3.21. कर्मादिभ्रतिः॥

The stronger amongst the third and ninth houses ini-
tiates the Shoola dasas for younger brothers.

Note: Karma = 51/12=3. [| feel that this should be
used for all younger co-bomns

2.3.22. प्रात्रदिर्भगिनीपुत्थोः॥

The stronger amongst the fifth and eleventh houses `
initiates the Shoola dasas for sisters and children.

Note: Matra = 65/12/=5; The sage uses the fifth for
sisters as it 15 the 3rd from 3rd. However, 1 feel that this.
should be used only for children.

2.3.23. व्ययादिर्ज्यैष्ठस्य॥

The stronger amongst the eleventh and fifth houses
initiates the Shoola dasas for elder brothers and sisters.

Note : (Vyaya =11). The eleventh rules elder co-born
and friends. :

2.3.24, पिततवतत पितृवर्गे॥

All paternal relatives are governed by the same shoola
dasa as that for father (vide earlier stanza 2.3.19).

## Page 212

2.3.25. मातृवत्‌ मातुवर्गे॥
All maternal relatives are governed by the same shoola
dasa as that for mother (vide earlier stanza 2.3.20).

Note : (1) Stanza 2.3.18-25 gives various Shoola dasas
for the native, brothers, father, mother, relatives, spouse
- etc. The principle involved is that the Shoola dasas are
always initiated from the 1st/7th signs from the houses
governing the person concerned. For examplé, the 5th rules
children. Hence the shoola dasas begin from the 5th house
or the 11th house (7th from 5th). Similarly, if the query
` relates to pet animals or servants, the Shoola dasas from
the 6th house (or 12th) should be used.

(11) Case studies using Shoola dasas can be seen after
~ chapter 11 Quarter 2.

2.3.26. ब्रह्मादिः पुरुषो समा नाथान्ताः।॥

Brahma dasa commences from the sign occupied by
Brahma and proceeds zodiacally if the starting sign is an odd
sign. The period of Brahma dasa is reckoned from the dasa
sign to the sign occupied by the lord of the sixth from it.

Note: ©) The Brahma dasa is another Ayur dasa
` ‘mentioned by Jaimini. The reckoning of Brahma planet is
such that it must occupy an odd sign. It is only in excep-

, , {jonal circumstances, when all the competing planets are in

even signs that Brahma will occupy an even sign.

(ii) dasa = 78\12 =6; The dasa period for any sign is
the number of signs (in years) intervening between the
dasa sign and the Lord of the sixth house from it. For
example, if Leo rises and Brahma is in Libra, the dasas
"will be regular and zodiacal from Libra. The sixth house
from Libra is Pisces and if its Lord Jupiter is in Gemini,
the dasa of Libra shall be for eight years. (Count from
Libr to Gemini minus one). `

2.3.27. स्थान व्यतिकरः

progress in the reverse direction

Note: (i) Sthana ना; Thus the seventh sign from that

2.3.29. पंचमे पदक्रमात्‌ प्राक-प्रत्यकत्वं चरवशायाम्‌॥

The progress of the Chara dasas (starting from the
ascendant / 7th house) would depend on the sign in the
ninth house being odd-footed (vimasapada) or evenfooted

(samapada).

Note : (i) Panchame =561/12=9; The chara dasa are
phalita dasas and are always regular. They commence
from the ascendant or the seventh house, which ever is
stronger. If the sign in the ninth house (reckoned zodiacally)
` is odd footed (vimsapada) the dasas will progress zodiacally
and if evenfooted (samapada), they progress in the reverse.

2.3.30. अत्र शुभः केतुः॥
Ketu is a benefic.

Note : For most purpose including the Chara dasa
etc, Ketu is a first rate benefic as it is always opposed to
Rahu (that eclipses the Sun). In fact, Ketu is one of the
Karakas for the upapada and should not be placed in the
second from it . During the period of the sign occupied by
Ketu marriage takes place and auspicious results are felt.

The dasa sign itself is the dwara (door)

Count as many signs from the dwara (door) as it has

Bahya (exterior)

2.4.4. तयोः पापो बन्थायोगादिः॥ |
If malefics are both in the door (dwara) and exterior
(bahya) signs, bondage and disease are indicated.

Note: The door is the sign though which the native in-
teracts with the external environment. If both the door and
the exterior are symbolised by evil signs and planets disease
and problems set in. However for bondage specific combina-
tion must exist in the chart vide stanza 1.3.42.

2.4.7, पितृलाभप्राणीतोऽयम्‌॥

The stronger between the ascendant and the seventh
house shall initiate the Narayan dasa (alias Padakrama
dasa)

Note: (i) This dasa is the hallmark of the Jaimini
Sutras and is, in my opinion, the best for all predictive
purposes. The stronger sign between the ascendant and the
seventh house as per the sources of strength vide chapter
IL. Quarter 3 shall initiate the Narayana Dasas. Narayana in
derived from the words ‘Nara' meaning native/self and
'Ayana’ meaning goals/direction. Parasara teaches that the
Supreme God Narayana by viftue of preponderance of a
Guna has manifested in three forms. With Satwa guna He
is Visnu, with Rajas Guna He is Brahma and with Tamas
Guna He is Siva. Accordingly the signs (symbolising
Narayana) were divided into three types viz. dual, movable
and fixed to represent Satwa, Rajas and Tamas respec-
tively. What would be the order with each of these three
types ascending is explaified in the subsequent stanzas.

(i) The direction of the dasas will depend on the sign
` In the ninth house been Samapada/Vimsapada.

2.4.8. प्रथमे प्राक्‌ प्रत्यक्त्वम्‌॥

will be regular.

2.4.18. सिद्धा उडुदाये॥।

2.4.19. जगत्तस्थुषोरर्था योगार्धो॥।
The periods of the signs in the Yogardha dasa is the
average of the periods of the signs in Chara & Sthira dasas.

Note: (i) Yoga is 'Union' implying addition of the
years obtained in Chara dasa system and Sthira dasa and
'Ardha’ is half, thus implying division of the sum by two
to obtain the period of Yogardha dasa.

(i) Parasara:

“Fmd च दशामानं द्रयोर्योगार्धसम्मिमत्‌।
लग्नसप्तमप्राण्यादिरदर्शय च प्रवर्तते।।*'

The periods of the signs of the Yogardha dasa is
the average of the periods obtained from chara and sthira
dasas for the sign. The dasa commences from among the
ascendant / seventh house whichever is stronger and their
‘adarsa’ sign and will be zodiacal /reverse depending on
whether the ascendant is odd/ even sign.

The (Yogardha) dasa commences from the ascendant
or ‘adarsa’ sign whichever is stronger. It is regular
and zodiacal if the ascendant is odd and reverse if even.

Note : Parasara has an identical view. Determine
the stronger between the ascendant & seventh house.
Now compare this to its ‘adarsa sign' (fable 2.4: Adarsa

dasas are the same as Chara dasa. After the trines, the dasa

its trines and so on, The succeeding signs are reckoned

in odd or even :

2.4.26. घास-गैरिकात्‌-पली-करात्‌- कारकैःफलादेशः॥

The results (of the Trikona and other phalila dasa) are

dasa sign

Note: (i) Dhasa = 79/12 =7; Gaorikat =123/12 =3
Patni = 1 ; Karat = 21/12 = 9

2.4.27. ताराकींशे मन्दाद्यो दशेशः॥

The Lagnadi Rasi dasa (also called Rasi dasa)
is explained. The birth constellation should be divided
into twelve parts, and the number of parts

(including fraction thereof) gained by the: Moon

should be converted into signs (degrees & minutes) and
added to the longitude of the ascendent to obtain Shri
Lagna.

Note: (i) ‘Tara’ means Janma Naksheira or
birth constellation; ‘Arka’ means the Sun and implies
the number twelve representing the twelve Sun
signs ; ‘amsa’ means portion/division . Hence 'Tar arkamse
means Nakshetramsa or Bhamsa which is the 1/27th
portion of a sign and 1/12th portion of a constellation
Manda = 1, implying ascendant and ‘adya’ means ‘increase
by’.

The arc traversed by the Moon in the birth -
constellation should be divided by 1320 (standard arc
of a constellation in Vedic astrology) and multiplied by
12. The result be converted into signs, degrees & minutes
and be added to the ascendant to obtain Shri Lagna
Readers may refer to the explaratory notes for a few
examples

If the Lord of Shri Lagna (or dasa rasi) is in own sign/
friendly sign the natives wealth & fortune are correspond-

middle class. :

2.4.30. दुर्गतो अपरथा॥
If the Lord of Shri Lagna (or dasa rasi) is in an
inimical sign, the native is poor.

Note : (i) If the Lord is a natural benefic and is
inimically placed, the native belongs to the lower middle
class. However if it is a malefic inimically disposed in a
malefic sign, utter poverty is caused .

(ii) The progress of the Rasi dasas indicates the
changes in fortune. These are subsequent to the
natural status indicated by the lord of Shri Lagna. A
radical change in status is possible if the lord of the
Shri Lagna aspects its sign of exaltation or the
ascendant

2.4.31. स्व वैषम्ये यथास्वं क्रम व्युत्क्रमौ!।

If the Shri Lagna is in an odd sign, the Laganadi Rasi

' ग the dasa sign is in an odd sign, the sub-periods will be

regular. x

2.4.33. शनौ चेत्येके॥

If Saturn is in Shri Lagna or dasa rasi, the progress of
the Rasi dasa / antardasa shall be zodiacal (even if the
signs involved are even signs ).

Note: Similarly if Ketu is in Shri Lagna or dasa rasi,
the progress of the Rasi dasa/ antardasa (as the case may
be) shall be reversed. This is an important rider.

2.4.34. अन्तर्भुक्त्यंशयोरेतत्‌॥
The antardasa (subperiods) and bhuktis (Sub-sub-peri-

ods) commence from the Lord of the dasa sign or its

seventh house . and are as per the preceding stanzas.

Note: This system of antar & bhukti reckoning is
used in all phalita dasas . .

EXPLANATORY NOTES:

In the third quarter Jaimini has explained some impor-
tant ayur dasas and one phalita dasa. The ayur dasa are the
Navamsa dasa, Shoola dasa, Sthira dasa and Brahma dasa
whereas the phalita dasa is the Chara dasa. Subsequently in
the fourth quarter the sage expounds the Narayana dasa
(Padakrama), Atmakarak Kendradi dasas, Manduka dasa,
Niryana Shoola dasa, Yogardha dasa, Drigdasa, Trikona
dasa & Lagnadi Rasi dasa (Sudasa). Some of these dasa
have many variations and the applicability has not been
indicated. To add to the multitude he says that other dasa
system including the host of constellation based dasa should
be learnt from standard texts.

2. The point is that no single dasa system can be a
final say in astrology as the various influences are blended
into the life of the individual. The Navamsa and Shoola

---

## Page 230

/
i

220 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

dasas enjoy a prime place among the ayur dasas, but

.. suffer from a limitaion of the upper longivity ceiling at

108 years. I have already given a detailed exposition
of using shoola dasas for predicting the death of father,
mother, spouse etc. in an earlier chapter. A few more case
studies have been taken up to appreciate the genius of
Jaimini

3. The sage teaches four important sources of strength.
~ These sources are independent of each other and are used
. for distinctly different purposes . Hence a. mathmetical
model that attempts to consolidate these strength is undo-
-ing 106 Jaimini Sutras. The First Source of stregth is used
for all purpose to compare the strength of two signs like
1st/7th or the signs occupied by the two eighth Lords etc.
7111658 otherwise specified this is generally used. The
Second Source of strength 1s the aspect of atmakrak, Mer-
cury, Jupiter and the Lord of the sign and is exclusively
used in Navamsa dasa, Chara dasa & Narayana dasas. The
Third Source of strength is seen from the position of the
Lord of a sign in occupying a quadrant, succeedant or
preceedent from the atmakarak or lagna. This is normally
“used for Atmakrak Kendradi Rast / Graha dasa,
. Lagna Kendradi Rasi / Graha dasa etc. The Fourth
Source of strength is the aspects /conjunction of malefics /
Rudra etc. This gives strength to the sign to
inflict death and is used in all ayur dasas. ` Thus
these sources are exclusive of each other and can not be -
clubbed

Selection of Brahma : Determine the stronger be-

petitor succeeds and becomes Brahma. However stanza
2.1.50 applies and the sixth planet from Saturn viz. Mars
becomes Brahma (even if placed in an even sign since this
is a case of transfer of function). :

(c) Brahma Dasa : Let us calculate the Brahma das
as of Sri Rajiv Gandhi (Chart 48). As estimated earlier,
Mars is the Brahma planet and is placed in virgo (even
sign). Brahma dasa, in exceptional cases when the Brahma
is in an even sign, commence from the seventh house and
progress in the reverse. Hence the dasa commences from
Pisces and progresses in the reverse direction in the order
Pisces- Aquarius-Capricorn-saggitarius.

It maybe noted that the method of counting has
been explicitly stated by Jaimini as direct for odd signs
। and reverse for even signs. (odd footed/even footed does
not arise in Brahma dasas as the method of determin-
` ing Brahma itself relies only on the nature of the sign
as odd/even.)

Pisces is an even sign and the sixth house (counted in
the reverse® is Libra whose lord Venus is in the eighth
from it in leo. Hence the dasa period of Pisces is seven
(8-1) years. Aquarius is an odd sign and the sixth house
(counted zodiacally) is Cancer whose lord Moon is placed
in the seventh from it in leo. Hence the dasa period of

---

## Page 238

` 228 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

Aquarius is six (7-1) years, The dasa periods of other
“signs have been shown in the adjoining table for Brahma
dasas for chart 48. However it maybe noted that for
` Virgo (even sign), the sixth lord Mars is in Virgo and as
per Chara dasa reckoning this should have given 12 years `
` (13-1), but in Brahma dasa this gives a zero period (1-1)
in the first cycle. Longivity normally extends from

Chara Dasa Of Gen Franco : Chara dasas begin
from the Lagna/Seventh house whichever is stronger and in
chart 49 (General Franco) the ascendant with two planets is
$tronger than the seventh house. The ninth house is Gemini
which is a Vimsapada sign indicating that the dasas will be
zodiacal. The order as determined shall be Libra-Scorpio-
Saggitarius.... The Lord of the Libra, Venus is in Libra and
hence gives a period of 12 years (13-1). Scorpio dasa is
obtained by counting directly (vimsapada) from it to Libra
to obtain 11 years (12-1). Saggitarius 15 a vimsapada (odd
footed) sign and its lord Jupiter 15 in the fourth from it |
(counted directly). Hence the period of Saggitarius is 3
years (4-1). Capricorn is a samapada (evenfooted) sign and
its lord Saturn is in the fifth from it (counted in the
reverse). Hence the period of capricorn is 4 years (5-1). In
` this manner the period of chara dasa of all the signs can be
determined (see adjoining table). For Cancer, the moon is
£ 11९५ and hence the dasa period of 2 years (3-1) 15
increased to 3 years. है

In this manner the dasas can be calculated and
longivity/life events or trend predicted. However readers
may note that the chara dasas are normally applicable for
chara (movable) ascendants. Similarly the choice of Ayur
dasa should be made carefully by an intelligent and initi-
ated ashologer. I have explained a few 08585 and leave it to
“the readers to learn the rest. The Narayana and Sudasas are -
the best and are like the Vimsottari and Ashtottari of the
Nakshetra dasas. These are universally applicable. Drig
Dasas are used from spiritual purposes (Dharma) while
Manduka Dasas are used in Rudramsa The Atmakarak
kendradi Rasi/Graha Dasas should be used only in the
charts of kings and persons in power.or where the
Atmakarak is involved in Rajyoges/ Pravrajya Yoga, while
the lagna kendradi Rasi/Graha dasas find universal applica-
tion. T have not found much success with the Niryana
Shoola dasas and Yogardha dasas. In case of a divergeant
view, the learned readers may kindly enlighten the scribe.

the param ayur should be roughly estimated and then
distributed equally over the signs to obtain the shoola

A Lok Sabha is elected in India for a period of five
` years and this is the Param Ayus of the parliament and
hence, every swearing-in-ceremony chart should be given a
Param Ayus of 5 years irrespective of the expired period
since elections. Thus every Shoola dasa 1s for a period of

5 months and every antardasa for 127 day. .

The BJP Government was sworn in during Leo Lagna
and the longivity estimation is as follows:-

(a) Lagna Lord (Sun) + 8th Lord (Moon)-= Fixed +
Moveable = Middle life.
(b) Moon + Saturn = Movable + Dual = Short life
(c) Lagna + Hora Lagna = Leo (Fixed) + Scropio (Fixed)
= Short Life. :
Clearly the short life factors dominate showing a
maximum longivity of four dasas i.e. 20 months.

3.1.1. अथ राज-जनिताभ्यां योगे योगे लेयान्मेषाधिापः॥

+ A Rajyoga arises by the conjunction of the atmakaraka
and the pitrukaraka or the lords of the first and fifth.
houses.

Note : Raja is a synonym for the Atmakarak while
Janita means father or Pitrukarak (fifth charakarak) Rajyoga
implies authority, luxary and a good life style that comes
with it. The nature of the planets and signs involved will
be the determining factor

3.1.2, उच्च-नीच-स्वांशवती तादृश दृष्टिञ्च शुभ-मातृदृष्टे
यदि महाराजः॥
If the planets are exalted/debilitated or conjoining/
aspecting the navamsa lagna or in aspect to each other and/
or only aspected by benefics, Maharaja yoga arises.

Note : (i) Either or both the pairs of Atmakarak &
Pitrukarak or lords of the ascendant and fifth house could
be as follow :-

(a) Conjoined or both planets exalted or debilitated.
(b) In mutual aspect and aspected only by benefics.

(५) Conjoining or aspecting the lagna/Navamsa lagna
and placed in strength.

(ii) - Maharaja Yoga implies international stature.

If (the aforementioned Rajyoga/Maharaja Yoga) is in
the ascendant/seventh house, these will occur late in life.

If (the aforementioned Rajyoga/Maharajyoga) 15 in the
ascendant/7th house, the good forture promised is away
from birth place.

should planets in lagna give fortune in foreign places? In
fact if the 7th, Sth or 12th houses have yoga this occurs in
` 2 foreign place.

If Moon and Venus conjoin/aspect the places men-
‘tioned conveyances are obtained.

certain houses/planets have been referred to Some have
, interpreted Tatra (26/12 = 2) to mean the second house.

If the Rajyoga has the conjunction of Saturn or ketu,
elephants and horses join the entourage.

Maharaj Yogas. If the planets are in the second he could be
riding elephants for the king/Govt.

(or the ascendant), second or fourth houses Rajyoga `
occurs.

If the lords of the ascendant, seventh and ninth houses

ruling self, partner and fortuné are involved and the strenght
of the lords in also vital for the Rajyoga.

If these Rajyogas (vide previous stanzas) occur in the

mutually aspect is the Rajya sthana (place of Rajyoga). In

these are easily attained early.

If the second and twelfth houses have equal number
of (beneficial) planets, Rajyoga is obtained

friendly signs, above average / average wealth is indicated.
, [0 inimical signs there will be very little wealth.

EXPLATORY NOTES:

` Jaimini has given various Rajyogas and Maha-
rajayogas which” are quite different from those
given in standard texts. Rajyogas caused by the
special ascendants have already been explained in an ear-
lier chapter and few case studies have been taken up
to examine the stanzas in this quarter. However before
declaring results, the divisional chars especially Navamsa,
Dasamsa and Panchmama should be examined. The
strength of the Luminaries decide strength and efficacy
of the Rajyogas. ।

Case Studies

Chart 53: EMPEROR AURANGZEB born on
3rd November 1618, 1:58' PM LMT at Delhi
(18:30'Ghati)

AURANGZEB
3RD NOV, 1618
1:58 PM LMT

NAVAMSA
®-9

Lagl6°15* Yup 9°26' (PuK) Sun 22°19'(AmK)

Ven 5°45 (GK) Moon3°39' (DK) ` 59 (R) 18°2'(MK),
Mars 16°20'(PK) Rahu 8°32'(BK) Merc 25°8'(AK)

Aurangzeb was the last of the Great Mughal emper-
ors of India. The lagna Lord Satum and fifth Lord Mer-
cury are in mutual aspect generating a Rajyoga as the
-Atmarkarak Mercury and Pitrukarak Mars are in mutual
aspect consolidating the Rajyoga. Added to this, Saturn
(Lagnesh) conjoins an exalted Moon that aspects the fifth
Lord Mercury. The Sun having obtained Neechabhanga
Rajyoga (exalted in Navemasa as Mars and Saturn are in
Kend:as to Lagna) also joins and aspect the Saturn &

---

## Page 254

244 Jaimini Mlaharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

Mercury. The association of the Royal planets in
strength to the Lords of the first and fifth houses generated
a Maharajayoga making him the emperor of India. To add
to the strength, the Maharajyoga occurs in the Arcodha
~ Lagna (Taurus) While the Sun gave him authority and
power, the exalted Moon assured vehicles & Luxuries.
The conjunction of Saturn and the aspect of Ketu
gave him many elephants and horses (stanza3.1.6).
The atmarkarak Mercury conjoins the Sun in the
ninth house and aspects the Pitrukarak (Mars) in the
seventh house and Jupiter in the ascendant resulting
in a Rajyoga (stanza 3.1.8) that gave him the peacock
throne studded with brilliant emeralds (Mercury).
However since there are equal number of planets in
Lagna (Jupiter) and seventh (Mars) the Rajyoga arises
later in life and after some struggle (stanza 3.1.9). Jupiter
is the eleventh Lord from Arudha Lagna showing living
elder brothers because of whom Aurangzeb could never
have become the emperor of India , while Mars is
. the Pitrukarak (father) who was quite opposed to
Aurangazéb and favoured the eldest. Jupiter is aspected by
Sun, Mercury and Ketu showing many elder co-born and
- Venus as the Lord of Arudha Lagna (responsible for
promoting status of the native) aspects the eleventh
house Pisces thereby destroying the elder brother. As
Rahu is in the ninth house from Arudha Lagna, he
enslaved his father in Agra till death. The killing of
वल brother resulted in the weakening of the Chara
Putrakarak (Jupiter) and the consequential decline
of the empire after him. (stanza 3.1.17) Auranzeb
has Moon in the fourth from Jupiter indicating
prosperity. However, Jupiter ultimately caused death
by his falling from a staircase as it is In Saggitarius
Navamsa.

PANCHMAMSA
D-5

The Panchmamsa (D-5) has a powerful Graha
Malika Rajyoga from the ascendant to the seventh house
where seven planets are involved including an exalted
Moon and Saturn in Capricorn. Rahu is well place in
Virgo showing the use of spies and informers extensively.
Since Mars initiates the Malika yoga the reign will be
marked by feuds and war and since the Sun terminates the
yoga the purpose will be for power or misuse of religion.
Four malefic planets in Kendras show Sarp yoga and true
to its nature the native was quite fanatical and destructive.

Chapter III. Quarter II

3.2.1. यज्ञ जनेशाभ्यां स्वकारकाभ्यां निधानम्‌॥

Death (of the native or others) is to be known from
the first and eight houses from the (concerned) ascendant/
house and Karaka. (significator) :

Note: (i) Yagna = 1, Jana = 8; The term 'Swakaraka
bhyam' indicates the 'Swa’ (Lagna/house) of Kara
(significator). Thus for the native, the first and eight houses
and their Lords form the ascendant and atmakarak are used in
timing death. In fact this stanza gives the finer details on how
to use stanzas 2.3.18 to 2.3.25. For example, if the death of
father/paternal relation is being examined, stanza 2.3.19 &
2.3.24 state that the shoola dasas begin from the 9th house or
seventh therefrom (i.e. the third house) whichever is stron ger.
The sign occupied by the fixed Karaka or its eighth house or
the Lords of these signs shall determine the death inflicting
shoola dasa for father. Now, for paternal relatives treat the
Chara Pitrukarak as Lagna of father and determine the house
of the relative. If fathers mother is under consideration, treat
the fourth from ninth i.e. 12th house and fourth from chara
pitru karak as her Lagna. Take the eight house and Lord from
this place and use the pitru shoola dasa to fix the fatality.

(ii) Some authors treat this as a separate method for
timing Longivity

---

## Page 260

250 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

3.2.2. निधानं लेय लाभयोःप्राणी॥ `
Death inflicting houses should be determined from the
first /seventh (from the bhava or Karaka).

Note: This has already been explained. e.g. The stron-
ger between ninth and third is used to initiate the shoola
dasas for father. The Lords of the eighth from the Sth
house (and its seventh ie. 3rd house) are called Pitru
` Rudra. Similarly the Lords of the eighth from the pitrukaraka
` and its seventh are also qualified as pitru Rudra. However
all four do not become Rudra; the strongest does.

` If Jupiter is in a quadrant, aspected by Saturn or Mars

or if Saturn is in the bhoga rasi of Jupiter, Kakshya hrasa

“(Longivity compartment reduction) takes place. ,

Note: Jaimini gives the finer details in these stanzas
` For example if stanza 2.1.10 & 2.1.14 are simultaneoustly
applicable the course of action has been explained here.
Thus, Jupiter in a qudrant aspected by Saturn / Mars results
in Kakshya Hrasa. Again, Jupiter will occupy some house
from the ascendant. Detremine the bhoga rasi for this sign
and if Saturn is placed therein, Kakshya hrasa occurs. The
principle in this stanza is that Mars and Saturn have evil
and obstructive influence on Jupiter leading to Kakshya
hrasa. :

The Moon in the eighth or twelfth house causes
reduction in Longivity (Kakshya hrasa).

by the methods in Chapter II Quarter 1 and is extended
to the Longivity estimation of parents and other
relatives. :

Note: (i) This is the Third Method of Longivity esti-
mation after the two methods given in Chapter IT Quarter
1. Some astrologers have clubbed this method with stanza
2.1.5 of Method 1, thereby creating unneccessary confusion
about seemingly differences of opinion between Panasara
and Jaimini.

(ii) Stanza 3.2.15 indicates that in this method the
Lagna and Moon are considered. The principle adopted
in this method is the same as Method I although it
seems to be different. If Lagna and Moon are both in
movable signs, the eighth houses (reckoned directly} of
both will be in fixed signs and stanza 2.1.4 teaches that
this indicates short life. Hence the sage has inferred
that if both Ascendant and Moon are in movable signs,
. short life is indicated.

(iii) Just see what happens if stanza 2.1.5 is inter-
preted as Ascendant and Moon. It would be in complete
contrast to this stanza. The principle adopted in the first
method is pairing of two factors one concerning the
ascendant and the other concerning the eighth house.
Thus, (a) Lagnesh & 8th Lord, (b) Moon (significator
of Head) and Saturn (Significator of 8th house) and (c)
Lagna & Hora Lagna from the pairs the first method.
This is in contrast to the third method where both the
factors concern the head i.e. Lagna & Moon.

Case Studies: . ः
CHART 55: CHARAN SINGH 23rd Decmber 1902,
7:23’am.; Near Meerut.

. CHARAN SINGH |

23RD DEC, 1902

SUN

Chaudhary Charan Singh had a very eventful political
career culminating as the Prime Minister of India. How-
ever, we are to examine longivity in this chart 55 by the
third method.

(a) Lagna + Moon = Dual + Dual = Long life.
There is no affliction to either lagna or the Moon by
Saturn.

(b) Lagna Lord + Seventh Lord = Jupiter (Movable) +
Mercury (Dual) = Middle life .

Lagna Lord Jupiter conjoin Saturn but this will not be
treated as an affliction since Saturn is in its own sign with
Jupiter (stanza 2.1.12). Besides, Mercury is conjoined by

the Sun in Lagna meriting increase of life span. (See notes
under stanza 3.2.22) to Long life. Thus, we may conclude `
~ that both (a) & (b) indicated long life (72-108 years).

The Navamsa dasas begin from the ascendant and
progress regularly.

The long life compartment is from Leo to Scorpio.
The Moon is in Virgo with Mars (see notes under stanza

---

## Page 271

Chapter Il Quarter II 261

3.2.24) and this sign attains maximum potential to end life.
Further, the eighth Lord is the Moon and is placed in Virgo
(stanza 3.2.27) He died in the dasa of Virgo (81-90 years)

in May, 1987 in his 85th year.

CHART 56: RAJIV GANDHI born 20th August 1944.

चुद No
Up

RAJIV GANDHI

20TH AUG, 1944

(a) The Lagna is in a fixed sign as the Moon is also in
a fixed sign showing middle life.

(b) Lagna Lord Sun is in a fixed sign as seventh Lord
Saturn is in a dual sign showing short life. The first pair
proved to be stronger and he lived upto 47th year.

Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
Atmarkarak : Venus.

(a) The ascendant is a fixed sign as the Moon is in a
movable sign indicating long life. Both are in Saturn nine
- signs and hence the affliction of Saturn does not arise.
However, the Moon is placed in the twelfth from the
ascendant (stanza 3.2.6) indicating Kakshya hrasa and long
life is reduced to middle life.

(b) Both Lagna Lord Saturn and seventh Lord Sun are
in fixed signs showing middle life span (36-72 years).

The shoola dasas begin from the ascendant and middle

life is covered from Gemini to Virgo. Both Gemini &

Virgo are aspected by atmarkarak Venus, and Jupiter and

. will not kill. Cancer is aspected by Mercury. However, Leo

“is aspected by Moon, Mars, Rahu, Ketu (see stanza 3.2.24)
and killed the native in its dasa (54-63years).

In the next quarter, Jaimini teaches about the nature of
death and the presence of Rahu in the eighth from
Atmarkarak (Venus) with Mars caused dustamarana yoga
resulting in his assasintion. A few examples will suffice to
show the usefulness of this third method of longivity
estimation. However, it should be attempted only if the
results of the first two methods are at variance.

3.3.1. लेय लाभयोः पवम्‌॥
The Aroodha padas of the ascendant and the seventh
house are being considered

Note (i) Leya = 13/12 = 1 Labha = 43/12 = 7 The
0202 of the seventh house is popularly called the Darapada

(ii) The Aroodha of the second house is called Kosa
pada, of the third Bhatru pada, of the fourth Matrupada, of
the fifth Mahatma pada or Mantrapada, of the ninth Bhagya
pada, of the tenth Rajya pada and of the twelfth Upapada.

3.3.2, पद भावयोश्चरे।।

If the eight house (or its lord) from the Aroodha
Lagna/Darapada is in a movable sign, dealth will occur in
a distant place.

Note : Bhava = 44/12 = 8 If the eighth lord is in
a movable sign, dealth is at a distant place, if in a fixed
sign, it is at home/near home and of in a dual sign
neither far away nor close or on the way. Similarly, if in
a fiery sign, the direction is east, if watery North, if
Airy-West and if Earthy the direction is south,

3.3.3. ब्रन्त राशौ कर्मणि दुष्टं मरणं॥
If the third house (from Aroodha Lagna/Darapada) is
a malefic sign, a bad/unnatural death occures.

---

## Page 274

264 ` Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

Note : (i) Karma = 51/12 = 3 : Stanza 2.2.12 is -
identical and advises examination of the third house from
lagna instead. Thus, the Arudha Lagna should be treated
as lagna for most purposes.

(ii) Similarly stanza 2.2.13 can be extended here
to imply that if the third house is a beneficial sign a
normal death should be expected. Also stanza 2.2.14 for
mixed results if the sign is benefic but afflicted by
malefics or vice-versa

` 3.3.4. कर्मणि पापे राजाभ्यां यथा सनद्ध॥

। If malefics (like the Sun etc.) are in the third house
-the king (Government punishment) etc, shall be the cause
“of death.

Note : Karma = 3; ‘Rgjabhayam’ means king and
` others which Jaimini has already taught vide stanzas
2.2.15 (0 2.2.29. Thus Jaimini has avoided repetition of
all 15 stanzas on planets in the third house and advises
that these will also apply to the third from Aroodha
Lagna. However an intelligent application is necessary.
For example, the Sun (malefic) in the third in a beneficial
sign may indicate assasination for political purposes by
terrorists etc

3.3.5. विने दिनौ quam

The eighth house and the eighth from it (i.e. the
third house) from Arudha Lagna determine the period =
place and nature of death

Note : (i) Dina = 8 ; Dine Dinou = eighth from
eighth house i.e. third house; ‘Punya tithi’ means the date
of death and Punya implies details of death.

(ii) Punya also indicates the nature of the sign as
movable, fixed or dual which are called Punya, Pushkara

and Adhana rasis respectively.

The third from the eighth (i.e. the tenth house) also

“indicates the death.

previous stanza where the eighth house is under reference.

Thus, the first, eighth and tenth, houses and their lords
determine longivity and death.

(1) Parasara

Saturn are in quadrants, trines or the eleventh house, the

‘native is long lived.

Vyankatesh Sharma : (Sarvarth Chintamani)

If the lord of tenth house is placed in friendly, own

or exaltation sign it confers long life. Similarly the
location of the tenth, first and eighth house lords in

, quadrants ensure long life.

Vaidyanath Dikshita : (Jataka Parijatha)

| आयुर्दायमनिष्ट हेतुमुदव्योमायुरी शकंब्जै।

## Page 276

266 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

While Ayurdaya has already been given, longivitiy is
again being discussed in connection with the eighth house.
The longtvity and health are determined by the lords of
the first, tenth, eighth houses and Saturn. If the lords of
the first, eighth and tenth are all strong (in quadrants,
trines or eleventh or exalted etc.) and unassociated with
Saturn, the native has long life. If two of these are
strong, the native has middle life and if only one is
shong, short life. The life will be very short if all three
are weak. Thus, this is the FOURTH method of longivity
estimation given by Jaimini.

` in the eighth death will not occur (during the period of

Note : The importance of the Charakarakas
(temporary significators) has been stressed in averting
death during the periods of signs where they are stationed
or aspect. Thus, during the Shoola dasas for self, the sign
having Atmakarak will note kill the native. Similarly the
sign having Darakarak will not kill the spouse. Instead,
the fixed significators (Sthira Karakas) can cause death
during their periods. For example the Sun/Venus as fixed
significator can kill the father during the Pitru shoola
dasa of the sign housing it whereas the chara pitrukarak
(temporal father significator) will tend to protect the

~ father

(ii) The principle (second) involved in this stanza

should also be considered in the lines of stanza 1.2.2 to
1.2.13. Thus, if the moon in the eighth house indicates a

from insects in the water should be anticipated (stanza

should be anticipated (stanza 1.2.9).

3.3.32, रोग मातृ दृष्टयोभवि मूषकादिना मूतिः॥

12 = 5 (Leo). | `

(ii) Let us examine this stanza from the first
principle explained under stanza 3.3.29. If Gemini is the
A.L./AK. and the Moon is in the eighth house in
Capricern, it aspects both Leo and Scorpio thereby
satisfying the conditions in stanza 3.3.32. ` The fourth
house from the Moon is Aries and vide stanza 1.2.2.
danger from mice and cats should be anticipated. Similarly,
if Virgo is the A.L./A.K. and the Moon is in the eighth
house in Aries, it aspects Leo & Scorpio satisfying the
criteria in this stanza. Thus, the fourth from he moon i.e.
Cancer indicates danger from creatures in water (stanza
1.2.5).

(iii) Thus in four stanzas Jaimini explains two
principles that are used for predicting the cause of death.
The third point is that the Moon normally indicates death
through living organisms/creatives. :

3.3.33. स्वांशो ग्राहां वर्ण नामभिः॥ |

Note : (i) Varna=54/12 = 6; Nama = 50/12 =

(ii) The second principle (vide stanza 3.3.31) is

indicate the death on the basis of stanzas 1.2.2 to 1.2.13.

Scorpio navamsa. However, the second and sixth from
Scorpio i.e. Saggitarius/Aries respectively could cause

(iii) Some interpret ‘Varna’ as Caste and ‘Nama’ as
name. While a death due to snakebite/poison can be
predicted if other conditions agree, 10 even attempt to
name the snake as a Cobra or Rattler would be hazardous.
Additional hints on the navamsas have been given in the
following stanzas.

(iv) Why are the second and sixth signs from the
navamsa of -the planet in the eight house considered?
Treat the navamsa of the planet as the eighth house. Then
the second from it is the 9th house and sixth from it is
the ascendant from matters pertaining to death. In this
manner the intelligent astrologer can appreciate the Jaimini
sutras

river, stream etc and in a dual navamsa it will be a large
expanse of water like a tank, sea etc.

Note : In movable navamsas or with Mars/Saturn
landslides and earthquakes are indicated and if with the
Moon, water/snow/ice/glacier is indicated as the cause of
death. In fixed navamsas trees are indicated as the cause
(moola division). If in Saggitarius navamsa the native
may fall from a tree to his death

3.3.53. शुक्रेण शुक्ल मेहात्‌॥

If Venus is in the aforementioned navamsa,
spermatorrhea & urinary problems (or diseaes in the
private parts) could cause death.

Note : Spermatorrhea is caused by Saturn’s affliction
(depletion) of Venus while Mars afflicting gives sores and
boils in the private parts (Syphyllis, Gonorrhea etc). The
affliction by Rahu gives dangerous diseases like AIDS
while that of Ketu damages the Scrotum. The affliction
0४ the Sun shows loss of fortune due to excesses. In this
manner the intelligent astrologer can divine the exact
results of placement of Venus in the death inflicting
navamsa/2nd/6th.

3.3.54. शनिना विष भक्षणादिभिः।।

If Saturn is in the aforementioned navamsas {6 ` `

- native consumes poison (Or poisonous substances).

3.3.55. राहु केतुभ्यां विष सपं लोष्ट्‌ बन्धानादिभिः॥
ः If Rahu or Ketu is in the aforementioned navamsas

` poison, snakes, flying objects, bondage etc could cause
death

Note : The association/aspect of Saturn/Gulika

---

## Page 289

Chapter II Quarter [I 229

confirms poison as the cause of death while the Sun's
- association/aspect confirms snakebite. Mars associating/
aspecting shows accidents (with moving object like vehicles
“or a missile etc.)

` 3.3.56. शनि राहुभ्यां राहुणा दण्डादिभिः॥

If Saturn and Rahu are in the aforementioned
navamsas death is caused by clubs (or other such weapons)
after being overpowered by enemies/evil people.

3.3.57. तत्र गुसराहूभ्यामभिचारादिभिः॥
If Jupiter and Rahu are in the aforementioned
pavamsas death is due to black magic, withcraft etc.

3.3.58. तत्र गुरुशनिभ्यां दृष्टे यथा स्वं नाशः॥

If Jupiter and Saturn are in the aforementioned
.. navamsas both the evil doer (attacker) and the native are
killed.

3.3.59. स्व त्रिंशांशे कौलकानां फलानि रोगादयः॥ `
Diseases and other evil are seen from the Lagna,
Trimsamsa and Kauluka.

Note : (i) By Lagna the sage refers to Drekkana
Lagna (D-3 Chart). Planets having the same drekkana
(movable/fixed/common) as Lagna shall afflict the portion
above the neck. Planets in the second type of drekkana
from Lagna afflict the trunk and in the third type, they
afflict the Lower portion of the body. For example, if the
ascendant is in a movable decanate, all planets in movable
decanates influence the head (above the trunk and planet
in common decanates influence the Lower portion of the
body. :

Again, by Lagna, the sage also refers to the -
ascendant and twelve houses which rule various parts of
the body (Chapter IV. Quarter [ gives details)

---

## Page 290

280 =. `. Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

(ii) Kauluka is Shastamsa i.e. one-sixth division of
a sign into equal compartments of 5० each. For odd signs
the Kaulukas are reckoned from Aries and for even signs
from Libra. (Table 3.2). If disease of a particular type
- (say blood problems) are indicated in the trimsamsa
(D-30 Chart) these will show up during the periods of
planets/signs in the particular kauluka from Lagna (for
blood problems the third Kauluka from Lagna should be
seen).

~ (iii) The trimsamsa refers to the degrees of a sign

~ that are grouped under the five planets ruling the five
tatwas (primordial elements/state of matter & energy).
For odd signs these are Mars (5°-Fire/Energy), Saturn
(5°-Earth/Solid) Jupiter (8°-Sky/Vacuum), Mercury
(7°-wind/Gaseous state), Venus (5°-Water/Liquid state).
Table 3.3 gives the trimsamsa (D-30).

Some commentators feel that Jaimini’s Trimsamsa is
different from that of Parasara. However, Jaimini has
categorically referred to the standard texts (including
Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra) for the various divisional
charts etc (Stanza 1.1.35)

3.3.60. ललाटे प्रथमम्‌॥
If (the afflicting planet is) in the first Kauluka the
disease/injury will be in the forehead

Note : In the stanzas 3.3.60-65 Jaimini explains how
a planet that shows disease/evil in the trimsamsa chart
and is also placed in Lagna drekkana causes ailments
when in specific ‘Kaulukas’ (i.e. compartments). Since
this portion relates to neck and above, such results are
explained. These should be extended to each of the six
portions of the trunk/lower body on the basis of the
drekkana.

3.3.61. केशो द्वितीयम्‌॥

If (the afflicting planet is) in the second Kauluka
there will be disease in the hair.

3.3.62. रुधिरं तृतीये॥
If (the afflicting planet is) in the third Kauluka blood
disorder/disease may result

Note : (i) Blood disorder/disease could mean anything
from blood pressure to blood Cancer. In the previous two
stanzas Jaimini explained the first principle behind the
Kaulukas as the specific parts of the body on the basis of
the drekkana. Thus, the third Kauluka can also indicate
diseases of the ears.

(ii) In this stanza Jaimini explains the second principle
on the use of kaulukas. These will be Lorded by the
planets in the order of weekdays from Sun to Venus.

---

## Page 292

282 + "Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

The third Kauluka will be Lorded by Mars ruling the
blood. Thus, a disease causing planet in the third Kauluka
will also indicate blood disorders

3.3.63. चतुर्थे नेत्रे।।
If (the afflicting planet 15) in the fourth Kauluka eye
disease results.

3.3.64. सिंहादिभिः पंचमे
If (the afflicting planet is) in the fifth Kauluka
danger from wild cats & Lion exists.

Note : In this stanza Jaimini develops the third
principle on the use of the Kauluka as the sign, counted
from Aries or Libra, could indicate the trouble. In this
stanza the fifth Kauluka is referred to and the fifth from
Aries (Leo) will indicate the trouble (stanza 1.2.6) as
danger from tigers, Lions etc. The Kauluka chart should
_ be drawn for this purpose.

3.3.65. षष्ट जिहवाग्रे॥

If (the afflicting planet 18) in the sixth Kauluka
diseases of the tongue (mouth/throat) could result.

3.3.66. पूर्वं षट्के राहु केतुभ्यां स्वे जिहवादिभिः॥

The results of the previous six stangas should be
applied for Rahu & Ketu from the tongue onwards (in the
reverse).

Note : In the notes under stanza 3.3.59 it has been
explained that the reckoning of kauluka for Rahu/Ketu is in
the reverse from the end of the sign. Thus, for example,
Rahu in 26° will be in the first Kauluka (25°-30¢
compartment) instead of the last and will afflict the forehead
(first Kauluka) instead of the tongue (last Kauluka).

3.3.67. तत्र शनिमाद्दिभ्यां गल द्वारादिभिः॥

If (the afflicting planet or its Kauluka) associates
with Saturn and Gulika the entire food tract from the
mouth downwards is susceptible to disease.

Note : By ‘Tatra’ Jaimini refers to the previous
stanza where the afflicting planet and its Kauluka are
under consideration.

3.3.68. तत्र कुजे शोषः॥
If it (afflicting planet or its Kauluka) associates with
Mars consumption results.

3.3.69. तत्र खौ प्रतिबन्धः॥ ,

` If it (afflicting planet or its Kauluka) associates with
the Sun, constipation and blockage of the excretory
system (including kidney stones etc.) results.

Note : After explaining the effect of the Kauluka
Jaimini explains the affliction of these by malefics.

3.3.70. लाभांशे मरणम्‌॥
Death is seen from the Rudramsa (Ekadasamsa).

Note : (i) Some have interpreted this as the seventh
(Labha = 43/12 = 7) from Karakamsa. However Jaimini
has already reserved this place for spouse and other
females. In this stanza Jaimini has explained the concept
of the Ekadas Rudras (eleven Rudras) and the use of the
Ekadasamsa which is also called Labhamsa (D-11 Chart).
This was frequently used by the Tajaka astrologers. The
initiated astrologers called this the Rudramsa (eleven
divisions of Rudra, the destroyer).

` (ii) Reckoning of Rudramsa.

` Chapter TI Quarter IT ` 285

The Rudramsas' are always reckoned zodiacally and
every sign has eleven Rudramsas (ekadasamsas) of
2°43'38" arc. For Aries these are reckoned from Aries;
for Taurus they are reckoned from Pisces; for Gemini,
reckoned from Aquarius; for Cancer reckoned from
Capricorn; for Leo reckoned from Saggitarius and so on.
Table 3.2. gives the Rudramsas.

(iii) On the basis of the longitude of the ascendant
and planets the division occupied by them can be
ascertained and the Rudramsa chart constructed.

3.3.71. मागे मार्ग रिपुणां वैरि वर्गश्च।।

As the dasa (Manduka) progresses from the eleventh
to its eleventh (i.e. ninth house) and so on, the
evils befalling the native are seen from the inimical
divisions.

Note : 0) Marga = 35/12=11; “Marge Marge”
means the eleventh sign from the ascendant and the
eleventh therefrom i.e. the ninth house. This is the
movement of the Manduka dasa in the reverse direction
(See stanza 2.4.15 for more details). Thus, the Manduka
dasa is specifically meant for the Rudramsa. Evil results
and weaknesses surface during the periods of inimical and
malefic signs (divisions) Parasara recommends fixed
periods of signs as per Sthira dasa for Manduka dasa as
well.

(ii) ‘Ripu’ refers to the Shadripu’ or six weaknesses
of Kama (Desire), Krodha (Anger), Lobha (Greed), Moha
(Passion), Mada (Alcohol), Matsarya (Sex) ruled by
Mercury, Mars, Rahu, Ketu, Saturn and Venus
respectively

3.3.72. स्व वैषम्ये रिपुभि
During the dasa of the Lagna/Atmakarak (or its

adarsa sign, whichever is odd) the native is conquered by
his enemies/weaknesses (i.e. dies).

Note : This applied to the-third and eighth houses 85 _
well.

3.3.73 क्रूराश्रयबले रिहतः॥
Death could also occur during the strongest of the

“strength wherein the sign associating with a larger number
ण malefics gains the strength to kill (Stanza 2.3.17)

3.3.74. शम्यार णि aid
Death could also occur during the dasas of the sign
(in the Rudramsa) ruled by Saturn Mars and Rahu

` 3.3.75. भावेशाक्रान्त राशिस्थः॥ |
| Death could occur during the dasa of the sign (in the
` Rudramsa) occupied by the eighth lord or its Bahya rasi

Note : Determine the eighth lord from the ascendant
in the Rudramsa. The sign occupied by it could inflict
death. This is Rudra dwara (Door way of Death) count as

many signs from it as the sign has gained from the

ascendant. This is the Bahya Rasi or Rudra Bahya (The
exterior from where the Rudra enters). Death could also
occur in this sign. (Bhava = 44/12 = 8).

| If the Sun conjoin/aspects the death inflicting sign, a
` close confidant or family member is the cause of death.

If the Moon conjoin/aspects the death influcting
sign, this (death due to close confidant/family member)
will surely happen.

3.3.78. कुजेन ज्ञातिभ्य:॥
If Mars conjoins/aspects the death inflicting sign, a
relative is the cause of death

If Mercury conjoins/aspects the death inflicting sign
stomach disorder (vomiting, dysentry etc.) or disputes/
differences will be the cause of death

` ` If Jupiter conjoins/aspects the death inflicting sign
quarrels and fire can cause death

3.3.81. तत्र शुक्र रूपे॥

If Venus conjoins/aspects the death inflicting sign,
the opposite sex (e.g. love affair/rape) can be the cause of
death.

3.3.82. तत्र नौ विष भक्षणादिभिः॥
If Saturn conjoins/aspects the death inflicting sign,
consumption of poison will be the cause of death.

Note : In stanzas 3.3.76-82 Jaimini gives the effect
of different planets on the death inflicting sign in
Rudramsa. However, whether the results of the planet or
the sign shall predominate is given in the subsequent
stanzas.

3.3.83, स्वांशे अपि॥।
If the planet is placed in its own sign, then its result
(as given under stanzas 3.3.76-82) shall predominate.

“Note : In fact, there is no difference in the result
indicated by the sign and the planet as the sign is owned
by the planet. For example, Venus in Libra Rudramsa
will surely indicate death due to a love affair.

288 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

3.3.84. अन्यतराश्च॥ ।
If the planet is placed in a sign other than its own,
the results of the sign shall predominate.

Note : For example, if Venus is in Capricorn
Rudramsa and if death is indicated in Capricorn, it will
be due to the consumption of poison (immediate cause).
‘However, the issue leading to consumption of poison
maybe a broken heart (love affair).

3.3.85. स्वे उच्चात्‌ पतनम्‌॥ |
If the planet is exalted, then the sign will cause the
fall of the native.

Note : An exalted planet will not kill the native.

धि . Hence, if death is indicated, the sign will have to do so.

‘Patanam’ means fall’ and should not be literally
interpreted as falling down and, instead, implies causing
. death like ‘felling a tree’.

3.3.86. नीचाश्रये विपरीतम्‌ |
If the’ planet is in its debilitation sign, the results of
| the planet shall predominate.

Note : (i) Being in debility in Rudramsa in a death
~ inflicting house, the planet gains. potential to cause death.
Hence its results shall predominate over the sign.

(ii) For example, if Venus is debilitated in Virgo, a
love affair will surely cause the natives death instead of `
quarrels/disputes (Mercury).

3.3.87. तनु तनौ दण्डहरः॥

The sixth is the house of Punishment and the eleventh
(sixth from sixth) is the house of emancipation of the soul
(i.e. death),

---

## Page 299

Chapter II Quarter [आ 289

Note : Tanu = 6, Tanu - Tanau = Sixth from sixth
i.e. eleventh house. ‘Danda’ refers to the punishment that
one gets either in the hands of enemies or such persons in
the sixth house while ‘Hara’ refers to emancipation of the
soul or the death in the eleventh house.

(11) Some astrologers opine that the stanzas 3.3.87 -
3.3.108 refer to the Shastamsa because of the use of
‘Chittamsa’ (Chitta = 66/12 = 6) in Stanza 3.3.98.
Further stanzas 3.3.89 - 3.3.94 (only six houses) cover
all the relations/foes and that the seventh house is again
treated as the ascendant instead of spouse. The peculiar
treatment of second house as that of parents and fourth as
that of wife adds credibility and the scribe is inclined to
agree with this version.

(iii) The shastamsa is the one-sixth division of a sign
covering 5° of arc. For odd signs the divisions are
reckoned from Aries to Virgo and for even signs the
divisions are reckoned from Libra to Pisces.

3.3.88. तत्र भावविशेषाः॥

These houses (i.e. the sixth and eleventh) should be
specifically examined for adversities and ill health
(respectively).

Note : ‘Bhava’ could also be interpreted as the
eighth house, but his would render an altogether different
meaning. For example, the eighth from the eleventh is
the sixth house and this has already been fixed for
adversities and not death/ill health.

3.3.89. अघशवं निधानम्‌॥
"The death of the native is seen in the second house
(fourth from eleventh). :

Note : Agha = 40/12 = 4; ‘Sava’ refers to the self/
native. Thus the fourth from the eleventh i.e. the second

Planets in trines to the seventh from the concerned

, 117६5. The trines to the seventh will also be the trines to

, 12th from lagna will be in trines to the seventh house

from the sixth (ruling enemies). Thus, they could ruin the

enemy. However, in the fourth they also threaten the co-

borns/relatives while in the eighth they will threaten the
native and his parents (seventh from the second)

3.3.104. तत्र रविशनिभ्यां ओजे कूटराशौ युग्मे निर्णयः॥
If the aforementioned houses is an oddfooted sign
with Sun and Saturn, the evenfooted sign aspecting it
shall determine the disease

Note : By. ‘Tarra’ the sage refers to the preceding
stanzas where certain houses namely Ist, 6th & 8th from
Jagna/Karaka were under examination for determining
death/disease. Now the sage explains the impact of planets
by an example of the Sun-Saturn conjunction in an
- oddfooted sign in any of the aforementioned houses. `

Then, the evenfooted sign aspecting them shall determine
the disease. For example, if the Sun is atmakarak and is
‘placed in Aries ascendant with Saturn, Aries being an
oddfooted sign does not determine the disease. Out of the
three signs (Leo, Scorpio and Aquarius) aspecting it, both
Leo and Aquarius in the Sth/11th houses from Aquarius
are evenfooted and determine the disease, which, as per
Jaimini could be the Stomach (Stanza 4.1.7) and ears
(stanza 4.1.13).

3.3.105. धानपुखाभ्यां पादरोगः॥
If the evenfooted ` 51878 are the third/ninth houses
from lagna the disease relates to the feet

Note : Dhana = 9 : Sukha = 27/12 = 3 ; The ninth
house relates to the feet in the Jaimini sutras

3.3.106. तनु विक्रमाभ्यामङ्गुलिरोगः॥ .

If the evenfooted signs are the sixth/eighth houses
from lagna, the disease relates to the fingers.

Note : Tanu = 6, Vikrama = 524/12 = 8

3.3.107. तत्र केतुना ASEH `. , ।
If Ketu joins the said places, the native may lose a
limb

## Page 304

294 | ` Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

3.3.108. तत्र पापदृष्टे पादहीनः॥
If the same (combination in the last stanza) is aspected
by malefics the native loses his feet

Note : An example has been cited in the Suh &
Saturn conjunction. Similarly other planets will show
‘other problems.

3.3.109. अथ बलानि॥
The strength of signs (to kill) is being described.

Note : What is the need for Jaimini to give the
‘strength of signs to kill when this has already been given
in stanza 2.3.177 It is evident that an elaboration is
necessary as the comparision of strength is of the signs in
the divisions (Rudramsa and Shastamsa) that have been
described so far.

3.3.110. शुभ दृष्टेयोगानन॥
A sign associated with benefics is weaker.

Note : Association of malefics adds to the strength
of signs to kill (Fourth source only) while that of benefics
weakens their evil.

3.3.111. चर पर्यायेण॥
The strength of two signs will depend on the nature
‘of the divisions

Note : If both signs in the divisional chart
, 276 equally conjoined benefics/malefics or not
conjoined, then their nature will decide the

strength

3.3.112. प्राणिनि शुभयुक्ते॥ .
Since the natural strength of signs to do good increases
from movable, fixed to common signs, their strength

---

## Page 305

Chapter Il Quarter Il 295

(under the present context i.e. to kill) decreases from
“movable, fixed to common

Note : Thus a dual sign is weaker than a fixed sign
that in turn is weaker than a movable sign to Kill the
native.

3.3.113. राशिः बली भागे॥ ~
If the signs are still equally strong, the aspect of a
‘benefic reduces (25%) strength.

Note : Thus the sign aspected by more benefics is
unlikely to kill as the sign with fewer aspects has a higher
death inflicting potential. :

3.3.114. शुभवृष्टिः त्रिशूले॥
While choosing among the trines, the criteria of
aspect of benefics should be considered first.

Note : In stanzas 3.3.110 - 3.3.113 Jaimini gives three
‘criteria of (2) conjunction of benefics (b) nature and (©) aspect
of benefics, in that order. However for choosing the death
inflicting sign among the trines, the order is reversed. For
example, if the Rudra is in a particular sign, death can occur
in its trines. Now, to choose the particular sign, the ones
with more aspect of benefics is rejected.

3.3.115. अंशेन त्रिशूले वा॥
This criteria (of aspect of benefics) is also considered
in the Amsas (Shastamsa/Rudramsa)

3.3.116. भाव कोणाभ्यां निसर्गतः॥

If the signs are equally aspected by benefics, their
nature as movable, fixed or common (in the receding
order) shall determine their strengths,

3.3.117. आश्रयतो बलिष्ठः॥
However a sign having more malefics is the strongest.

3.3.121. एवं निधानं मातापित्रेः॥
Similarly the death of mother & father can be

assessed

Note : If the ayur dasas are in Rasi chart, treat the
fourth house as mother and ninth as father. The eighth

houses from these i.e. eleventh/fourth house respectively

and their lords will determine the death inflicting dasa.
Instead if the Shastamsa is used, the second rules mother
& father and eighth therefrom is the ninth house, & 9th
Lord and its trines could be dangerous for parents.

3.3.122. भौम्यांशश्च निवृत्तिकारकः॥
However, if the amsa (shastamsa sign) is owned by
Mars, mother will not die

Note : Mars is the karaka for mother (stanza 2.2.2)

## Page 307

father. Thus the shastamsas of the sthira karakas (fixed
significaters) do not kill their Karakatwa (signification).

3.3.123. नाथान्ताः संज्ञा स्युः॥
। The period of the ५2825 is from the sign to its lord
` (as per the chara dasa scheme)

Note : (i) The only dasa so far mentioned in this
quarter is the Manduka dasa in Rudramsa. The periods of
the amsas will be from the sign to its Lord as per the
chara dasa scheme. However others advocate for fixed
periods, which is correct. Hence this stanza gives the
periods for the Paryaya dasas.

(ii) Refer to stanza 1.1.28.

3.3.124. कर्मस्था चर पर्याये॥।
If the ascendant is a dual sign, Chara Paryaya dasas
are applicable.

Note : Karma = 51/12 = 3 (Dual). The Chara
Paryaya Dasas are also called Trikona dasas. Since these
stanzas come after the Shastamsa, the Gochara Dasa
(comprising of Chara Paryaya, Sthira Paryaya and Ubhaya
Paryaya) are also applicable in the Shastamsa. These are
Ayur (Longivity) dasas although some astrologers have
also been using them for Phalita Jyotisha.

3.3.125. भाग्यदारयोः स्थिरोभययोः॥
If the ascendant is a fixed sign, Sthira Paryaya and if a
movable sign, Ubhaya Paryaya dasas are applicable.

Note : (i) Bhagya = 2 (Fixed) ; Dasa = 4 (Movable).
The distinction of applying Chara Paryaya to Dual signs
and Ubhaya paryaya to Movable (Chara) signs may be
noted. The periods of this dasa are like the Chara dasa
scheme i.e. from the sign to its lord

## Page 309

` Chapter II Quarter IT 299

(ii) CHARA PARYAYA DASA : Also called Trikona
dasas, these are applicable for dual signs in the Ascendant
The strongest among the 1st, 5th or Sth house (Trines)
initiates the dasa. After the period of the trines, the dasa
progresses to the second house from the initiating sign
and its trines and so on. The reckoning of trines/2nd
house etc is zodiacal if the initiating dasa sign is Vimsapada
(odd footed), else it is reverse for Sampada signs. Table
3.5 gives the Chara Paryaya dasas.

(iii) STHIRA PARYAYA DASA : These are
applicable for fixed signs in the ascendant. The stronger
between the 1st/7th houses shall initiate the dasas. After
the dasas of the first & seventh houses from the initiating
sign, it progresses to the second from the initiating sign.
After the dasas of the second and eighth from the

initiating sign, it progresses to the third and so on. Table

3.6 gives the Sthira Paryaya dasas. The progress (0 the
second is zodiacal/reverse depending on whether the
"initiating sign is vimsapada/samapada.

(ivy UBHAYA PARYAYA DASA : These are
applicable for movable signs in the ascendant. Like the
previous two, after covering four signs in quadrants it
progresses to the second house. The basic difference is
that Sthira Paryaya covers two signs (Ist & 7th) before
progressing to the second, Chara Paryaya covers three
signs (151, Sth & 9th) before progressing to the second
and Ubhaya Paryaya covers four signs (1st, 4th, 7th &
10th) before progressing to the second. To emphasise this
point Jaimini uses the words ‘Bhagya (2), ‘Karma (3)’
and ‘Dasa (4)* to describe these dasas respectively. Had
these not been implied, Jaimini could have used ‘Leya
(1) to describe the dasas for Chara Lagna. The Ubhaya
Paryaya dasa commences from the strongest of the
quadrants and is like'Lagna Kendradi Rasi dasa. However

3.3.126. भाग्यकारकाभ्या पम्रडःगलप्रदम्‌॥
The second house from the significators (sthira
karakas) is condusive for good results

Note : Death is not seen from the second houses
from the fixed significators. Instead, in the Shastamsa,
these second houses have been indicated. Besides, the
Rudra rasis of the fixed significators have already been
explained

3.3.127. मूत्युः मृत्युषि॥

Death (normally) occurs in the third house (from
AK./AL).

Note : Mrityu = 3.

3.3.128. अनयरन्यथा।॥

If death is not expected in the third house from
Atmakarak/Arudha Lagna, other signs (aspecting these/
trines 19 Rudra etc.) may be examined.

3.3.129, भृत्तमन्यत्‌॥
There are other methods of Longivity estimation that
are not quite upto the mark.

Note : A host of mathematical models like
Naisargikayu, Amsayu, Pindayu, Ashtaka-vargayu etc.
exist that can be quite off the mark. The methods given
by Jaimini (and Parasara) in this book are very accurate.

Explanatory Notes :

In this quarter the sage gives the final touches on the

© nature and timing of death of the native and others. Since

he has already advised the use of standard texts for the

---

## Page 312

- 302 । Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

divisional charts charts which merit additional attention
(Trimsamsa, Panchamsa, Rudramsa and Kauluka or
` Shastamsa) have been explained. Jaiminis reference proves
the validity of the relevance of the Tajaka divisional
charts like Fkadasamsa; Panchamsa and Shastamsa. The
other charts like Astamamsa, etc require considerable
research.

2.Jaimini has given a very specific use for the
Mauduka dasa in the Rudramsa and has restricted the
Shastamsa to the Gochara Dasas (Paryaya dasas). The
Paryaya dasas, like Narayan dasas, are the exclusive
contribution of Jaimini although parts of these are found
in other texts. The Padanadhamsa dasa is a variation of
‘Narayan dasas while the Bhavamsa dasas (yet another
variation) is meant for divisional charts.

## Page 329

Note: (i) Ketvamsa has been interpreted as the Navamasa
sign occupied by Ketu (see stanza 4.3.42 also) in the lines of
'Lagnamsa'. Another interpretation refers to Aries Navamsa
(Ketu = 61/12 = 1) and is in lines of standard texts like Suka

Navamsa. However, Jaimint has given an example of a tran-
sit system (Gochar) popularly known as " Brighu transit” in
Vedic astrology. When the Sun transit any sign and occupies
a Navamsa of the sign occupied by Ketu it attains functional
exaltation to invigorate the chart.

(ii) This is applicable to male charts.

3.4.14. गुरु त्रिशांशे॥
Conception can occur from the eleventh to eighteenth
day from the begining of the menstruation.

Note: The Trimasamsa of Jupiter in odd signs are from
10-18° and in evensigns from 12-20°. A direct interpretation - `
of this stanza as the transint of the Sun in these degrees would
amount to saying that women can conceive only in these par-
ticular eight days in every month. Some astrologers have
adviced the use of Kaulukas. In odd signs Jupiter does not
own any Kauluka. Does that mean women cannot conceive
when the Sun is in odd signs?

The basic astrological concept is that Menstruation can
begin in any sign occupied by the Moon when it is aspected
by Mars as the Moon rules over fluids (blood) and Mars rules
over fire (bile). If the Moon is placed in an Anupachaya house
(1,2,4,5,7,8,9,12) from the ascendant, then only can
conception occur during the ‘biological month’. If the Moon
is placed in an Upachaya house (3,6,10,11) when the
menstration begins, conception cannot occur. Now, the Sun
transits one trimsansa (1°) in a day and from the begining of

---

## Page 330

320 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

menstrution the first five days are ruled by Mars (bleeding)
followed by Saturn ruling the next 5 days (6th-10th) indicat-
ing formation of tissue and the likelihood of conception is
very low. However Jupiter rules the next eight days (11th-
18th) and it is during this period that conception occurs as the
uterus can receive the egg. The next twelve days presided by
Mercury (7) and Venus (5) show the hardening of the walls
and destruction of tissue. Thus, the *Sun is Jupiter trimsamsa’
refers to the eight days from the eleventh in the biological
month where the lady can concieve Vaidyanath (J.P.sl. 3.17.
& 18) is of the view that conception occurs from the fourth to
the sixteenth day after meanstruation and has given specific
results for the same. :

Note: A perusual of stanza 3.4.39 to 45 will reveal that
Saturn as the Lord of the child has nothing to do with the
complexion. Instead, it is the planet conjoining Saturn that
determines the complexion. The stanza 1.4.23 to 1.4.27 may
be perused where in the same principle is used. If a planet
conjoins the Lord of the child, its result shall predominate
unless the Lord of the child is exalted / debilitated. However
for predicting the complexion etc. of the child from the
saptamsa, stanza 3.4.46 can be used where the Lord of the
saptamsa sign where in the Lord of the child is stationed shall
determine the complexion. The colors given by Jaimini are
those seen on human beings and are practical.

~ This stanza presupposes the strength of the Varnada Lagna
as given in the previous stanza.

(ii) Generally for the birth of twins the dual signs should
be involved in Rasi and amsa. The conjunction of the Lord of
. the third house with the lord of the ascendant also indicates
the birth of twins or more depending on the number of plan-
ets aspecting.

from Adhana Lagna, when afflicted by malefics produces de-

330 वि Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
EXPLANATORY NOTES:

In this quarter, Jaimin explains the method of verifying
the fertility and timing of conception,. This is followed by a
host of detail on the Adhana lagna which is based on the
moment of coitus. Since this data 1s hard to obtain, the dicta
which are based on very sound astrlogical principles, can be
applied to the fifth house from Lagna, Navamsa Lagna and
Saptamsa lagna. In the Saptmasa chart, the fifth should be
treated as the Lagna of first child, seventh as Lagna of second
child and so on.

Fertility has already been explained in Chapter 1 Quar-
ter 4 and some examples have been given at the explanatory
notes. A few more cases shall be examined in the basis of the
stanzas given in this quarter.

CASE STUDIES:

Chart 64: Male born on 7th August 1963 at 9:14'IST at
211 28, 84 छ0 1.

CHART 64
MALE 7TH AUG,
1963

Sun = Cancer (AS 3) Arudha pada of ninth from Sun = Saggitarius (6.59)
Arudha of 3rd from Lag = Virgo (A3) Arudha of 9th from Lag = Cancer
(49)

## Page 341

, Chapter III Quarter IV 331
Fortune :

The Arudha lagna in in Saggitarius with Mercury
Vargottama in the ninth house indicating fortune dur-
ing its periods (stanza 3.4.1&3.4.2.). During Saturn -
Mercury (Dasa - Antar : Vimsottari) the native had a
grand fortune through his father. ।

Fertility (i) (Stanza 3.4.4.-3.4.9): The Arudha of
the third from the Sun is Cancer (AS3) as the Lord of
Virgo (Mercury) is in Leo. The ninth from the Sun is
Pisces and its Arudha is in Saggitarius (AS9). Be-
tween Saggitarius and Cancer, the latter with two plan-
ets is stronger. The eighth house from Cancer does not
have the conjunction of Mercury & Venus Sun, nor is
the Sun in the twelth second sixth eighth or from it.
Hence the native is fertile. Two important points maybe
noted in his example : (a) that the Arudha padas of
both the third and ninth are not taken to examine
planets in the eighth house. Only the stronger among
the two is taken. If instead Saggitarius (AS9) was
also taken,the Sun would be in the eighth house and
infertility should be indicated under stanza 3.4.7.

(b) that Under stanza 3.4.5 the eighth from
Arudha pada should be considered for planetary
conjunction to determine infertility. Some astrolo-
gers opine that the Anudha padas themselves be con-
sidered. This will give a wrong reading as then the
Sun in Arudha pada should deny fertility. In fact stanza
3.4.5, etc require the placement of the Sun in the 2nd,
8th, 12th or 6th from the Arudha pada to deny fertil-
ity.

(11) The Arudha padas of the third and ninth house
from the ascendant are in Virgo and Cancer respectively
and Cancer is again the stronger with two planets. The

In chart 65 the Sun is in Libra and the Arudha pada
“of the third and ninth houses are in Pisces and Aries
respectively. Pisces is aspected by four planets including
Jupiter and is marginally stronger than Aries aspected by
two planets. The Sun in the 8th house from Pisces thereby
indicating infertility.

The Lagna is Leo and the Arudha padas of the third
and ninth houses are Leo and Cancer respectively. The
latter is stronger with two planets. Mercury and Venus are
not in the eighth house. The Sun is neither is 2nd, 6th,
8th nor 12th. Thus, fertility is indicated.

It may be noted that when the fertility indication from
the Sun and Lagna are variant, the Lagna will prevail.

---

## Page 343

Chapter III Quarter IV 333

Hence, this chart 65 is fertile. The native has two daughters.
In case of variance, if the Sun shows fertility and the ascen-
dant shows infertility, medical intervention is required. If both
Sun & Lagna shows infertility, there can be no cure.

; In chart 67, the Sun is in Taurus and the Arudha
, 79025 of the third and ninth from it are in Aries (AS3) and

from them denying conception. However from Lagna, the
‘Arudha padas of the third and ninth houses are in Aquarius
and do not deny childern. Infertility is only indicated from
the Sun, and as such is not confirmed by Lagna. The
system of Arudha padas from the Sun and Lagna is
only indicative and a final decision can be had only
` from the saptamsa chart. This can be confirmed by the
Readers by applying the rules to Chart 23 of Smt J.
Jaylalitha wherein the Rasi chart does not deny childern
but the Saptmasa clearly denys children. There are other
mathematical points like Kshetra and Beeja Sphuta which
can be applied for initial indication.

41.1. पितु दिनेशयोः प्राणी देहः॥

The physical body is denoted by the stronger of the
ascendant or the Sun.

Note: The Sun is the naisargika Karaka (natural
significator) of the ascendant and hence the stronger be-
tween the ascendant and the Sun shall indicate the body.

The natural Karakas of the twelve houses are (1) Sun
(2) Jupiter(3) Mars (4) Moon & Mercury (5) Jupiter (6)
` Saturn & Mars (7)Venus (8) Saturn (9) Sun & Jupiter
(10)Jupiter, Sun, Mercury and Saturn (11) Jupiter and (12)
Saturn. The strength of the ascendant and Sun sign are
vital to good health.

4.1.21. पित्रः प्राक्‌ काले॥ `

If the Pitrukaraka or Matrukaraka are in the visible
signs from Deha(ascendant\Sun) the bodily defects arse
` after birth.

Note: (i) ‘Prak’ refers to the visible houses (seventh
to twelfth) from the ascendant or Sun. If the temporary
significators of father or mother are in the visible signs,
bodily defects arise in due course of time. ‘Pitru’ includes
both father & mother Karakas.

(ii) By impilcation, if these are in the invisible portion
they do not show defects.

4.1.23. अशोणितो क्लीबश्च ॥ |
If otherwise, the child is either illegitimate or eunuch.

Note: If the Pitrukarak / Matrukarak do not join/
aspect the ascendant / Sun, the child will be illegitimate
provided Jupiter does not conjoin nor aspect the ascendant/
Sun Moon, nor do these occupy a division of Jupiter. Else
the child will be legitimate. If instead of Jupiter, Mercury
is associated, the child will be a eunuch.

4.1.26. वर्णं भेदाश्रयेण॥
The profession is seen from the sign occupied by the
lord of Varnada Lagna.

Note: ‘Varna bheda’ refers to the Varnada Lagna as
well as the caste system based on profession on which the
son naturally inherited the same professon as that of father
(feudalistic society). However, with professional diversifi-
cation, the influence of other planets and signs besides the
dispositer of the Lord of Varnada Lagna. should be consid-
ered. The Fiery signs represant kshatriyas (authority) and
indicate politicians (Leo), Armed forces etc (Aries) and

buteaucrats (Saggitarius). The watery signs represant
` Brahmanas (intellctuals etc) and include priests(Pisces),
, astrologers, Magicians, research scientists etc (Scorpio)
and doctors etc (Cancer). The airy signs represent Vaisyas
- (Businessmen) and include traders (Gemini), industrialists
etc (Aquarius) and other businessman(Libra). The earthy
signs represent the Sudras (workers) and include Labour
(Capricorn), Accountants etc (Virgo) and other workers
(Taurus).

## Page 356

346 , Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

Note: ‘Swa’ means ascendant or Atmakarak.

Moorti (65/12 = 5) means the fifth houses and Purushe
(621/12 = 9)means the ninth house. ‘Kala’ refers to ‘Rudra’
or God in the destructive aspect. The Hindu believe that
God creates (Brahma) , God preserves (Visnu) and God
destroys (Rudra) . Thus, men born with this combination
of Moon and Rahu in the ninth/fifth house will take upon
themselves the role of the destroyer. This is called ‘Shakti
, yoga’ in Vedic astrology.

4.1.55. तिर्यग्‌ दृष्टौ प्रायो निवृत्ति कारकः॥

If Cancer aspects (or if the Rahu/ Moon are in
Cancer) then, generally, the evil results will be
contained.

Note: Tiryag = 316/12 = 4 (Cancer). Cancer 15 sym-
bolic of creation and represants Lord Shiva (God as the
Universal soul and the overlord of all the Rudras). If
Cancer aspects or contains the Rahu/ Moon, the evil may
not crop up at all. However, if this does not happen then
obstruction to the evil is seen from Cancer because Cancer
is the sign of exaltation of Jupiter representing God. [This
aspect has been discussed in the horoscope of Adolf Hitler
etc.]

4.1.56. शूलेशयोः दारयोः शतयौद्यं TEER

Jupiter aspecting the second, eleventh or seventh houses
(from Lagna / Karaka) gives a good longivity of a hundred
years. । । :

Note: Shula = 35/12 = 11; Isa =50/12 = 2 ; Dara = 28/

12 = 4; The second, fourth and eleventh are the houses of

primary Argala (intervention) and Jupiter’s aspect on these
brings strength & life to the ascendant.

## Page 357

Chapter TV Quarter 347

-» Explanatory Notes & Case Studies

This quarter deals with a few basic concept in the
Vedic Astrology and have been given as they are quite
different from the views of other Vedic astrologers or else
they are not to be found in available texts. The body parts
attributed to the signs are original to Jaimini. While Parasara
has discussed the use of Varnada Lagna for longivity,
Jaimini has correctly used this for both self, co-borns etc.
as well as livelihood & status. Parasara has given the
results of the pranapada in various houses from the ascen-
‘dant while Jaimini adds the effects of signs in which the
pranapada is as well as that of planets from it indicating
that Pranapada should also be studied as a special ascen-
dant. :

One comes across hunderds of yogas in the standard
texts. The sage has discussed ‘Shakti yoga’ caused by the
combination of Rahu and the Moon and describes it to be
a very evil combination when occuring in the fifth or ninth
houses. Some astrologers believe this to be a yoga for
‘power’ and have extolled its potential. If occuring in the
fifth from Pranapada, it indicates great sorrow. If this is in
trines to the Lagna /AK it shows potential for great de-
struction ‘What is being destroyed is seen from the planets _
conjoining / aspecting this combination. If malefics conjoin
the Moon & Rahu, it shows a good person as the destruc-
tion of evil occurs whereas if Jupiter conjoins, a very evil
person is indicated as the destruction of all that 15 good and
divine (Jupiter)is indicated. Thus, the various combinations
given 10 standard texts should be understood and applied
with an intelligent mind.

` Note: This inherent strngth of odd signs to be more
evil is used in initiating the Ayur dasas. The Navamsa dasa
always begin from an odd sign. (stanza 2.3.1 &2.3.2 ).
Similarly, the sthira dasa always begin from the sign
occupied by Brahma (stanza 2.3.4) and Brahma is almost .
always in an odd sign (stanza 2.1.49) The Brahma dasa
also begin from the sign ocupied by Brahma (stanza2.1.55&
2.3.26). The Atmarkarak Kenadradi (Rasi) dasa & Lagna
Kendradi Rasi dasa which are Ayur dasas also begin from
the odd sign in quandrants to the Atmarkarak/ Lagna
(stanza 2.4.11) The Manduka dasa (in Rasi chart) also
starts from an odd sign in the Lagna / ‘adarsa’ (stanza
: 2.4.15). The Yogardha dasa is also initiated from an odd
sign (stanza 2.4.19 &20) Thus these are all Ayur dasas
(Longivity / other evils). The only exception to this rule is
the initiation of Shoola dasas, which could occur from
even signs as well inspite of being an Ayur dasa. This
exception has been allowed because the dasas for each
relative including the self starts from a different house.
Thus the Shoola dasas for father & younger co-borns will
be different from the Shoola dasas for self/ spouse. The
Paryaya dasa are also an exception to this rule.

(11) Conversely, Phalita dasas (fruits of present life)
` generally start frcm the Moon/Lagna, irrespective of
strengths. These include the various constellation based
dasa (udu dasa stanza 2.4.18), Narayana dasas, Sudasa,
Charadasa, Atmarkarak /Lagna Kendradi (Graha) dasa etc.

longitude of the sixth house (or its lord) should be de-

4.3.2. काल निर्णयादिभिः॥
The determination of birth time is on the basis of the
ascendant etc. at conception.

Note: (i) Natal Moon : Jataka Parijatha (111.43) Deter-
mine the number of dwadasamsas gained by the Moon as
well as the dwadasamasa sign of the Moon at conception.
Now vount as many signs (from this dwadasamsa sign) as
the number of dwadasamsas of the Moon to obtain the
Janma Rasi (Birth Moon) Birth Moon could also be in
trines to this sign. For example, in a conception chart, the
Moon was at Aquarius 29°1536"". Thus, the Moon gains
12 dwadasmasas and is placed in the dwadasmsa sign
Capricorn. Now, counting 12 signs from Capricorn, we get

---

## Page 378

368 = `.  Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

Saggitarius indicating that the Moon at birth will be in
fiery signs. The natal Moon was in Leo.

(ii) Natal Sun: Jaimini Sutra (Stanza 4.2.20- 4.2.23)
Determine the stronger between the sixth houses from the
ascendant and the seventh. Ad the longitude of the sixth
(or twelth) Lord to that of the ascendant (or Seventh)
house. The sign obtained is the Sodhya Rasi. For example,
the ascendant as conception was Capricorn 10°20°37". The
Sixth and Twelfth houses are Gemini and Saggitarius. The
‘former was stronger and its Lord Mercury was in. Aries .
26°37. Thus the Sodhya rasi is at Aquarius (9/10°20° + 0/
26°37" = 10/6°58") and Natal Sun would be in an odd sign
or the signs of exaltation / debility of Saturn, whichever is
the strongest at conception. The Natal Sun was in Aquarius.

(iii) The example cited is a real life case and readers
may refer to the research paper of Mr. R. Santhanam
‘published in his book 'Essentals of Hindu Predictive
Astrology’ (Sagar Publication).

4.3.5, अनुलिप्ताश्च।।

The Degrees ,minutes and second of the ascendant are
converted in to time equivalents to detemine the time of
birth.

Note: (i) Amsa’ in the present context means the
‘degrees’ of the longitude of the adhana lagna. If the adhana
lagna is a day signs (Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Aquarius,
Pisces), birth will be at night and if it is a night sign, birth
will be during the day. Having fixed natal Moon & Star,
the date of birth is known. Determine the day/ night

duration and multiply it to the ratio of the ascendant
longitude (irrespective of signs) to 30°. The result should

4.3.6. Tgaififa चतुः संख्यादिः॥
2.4, etc even numbers can be subtacted (or added) to

I vighati.

4.3.8, आद्यांशके॥

next higher number.(‘Adya’ means ‘increased’ ‘amsa’ means
portion)

(ii) In the example, the reminder was 7.4 and since it
has a fraction (0.4) it is increased to the next higher
number 8.
