4.3.14. नीचे दारांशकः॥
If (Lagna/ Hora Lagna is) in an even sign, count in
the reverse from Pisces to it

Note: (i) Neeche = 60/12 = 12 (Pisces) Dara has been
interpreted as female signs (Dara means wife); ‘dmsa’ in
the present context is the first division i.e. the sign it-self.
However by using this word, Jaimini also indicates that the
# 8111808 Lagna etc. can also be determined in the divi-
sional charts by using the Hora Lagna & Lagna divisions.
Extending this further, the aroodha padas etc can also be
obtained by treating each divisional chart as an independant
horoscope. This area requires research

(ii) Varnada Lagna : If Lagna or Hora Lagna is in an
३०५ signs, count regularly from Aries to it and if in an
ven sign, count in the reverse from Pisces to it . The |
igures so obtained are to be added if both Lagna & Hora
.agna is in an odd signs or both are in even signs. The
igures are to be substracted if either lagna or Hora lagna is
n an odd sign and the other is in an even sign. The nett
esult is to be counted regularly from Aries or in the
everse from Pisces depending on whether the Lagna is in
n odd or even sign respectively. The sign arrived at is the .
Jarnada Lagna. Similarly the Varnadas of the other houses
ire also to be determined

For example, if Lagna is Capricorn and Hora Lagna is
Libra count in the reverse from Pisces to Capricorn (even
sign) to get 3 and count directly from Anes to Libra (odd
sign) to get 7. Since Lagna (even) and Hora Lagna (odd)
are in different groups, we take the difference between the
figures (7-3=4). Since the Lagna is an even sign we count
four signs in the reverse from Pisces to arrive at Saggitarius

---

## Page 383

Chapter IV Quarter III 373
` which is the Varnada Lagna.

, astrologers opine that the longitude of the ascendant &
Hora Lagna are also to be used. If in the above example
the ascendant was Capricorn 17° and Hora Lagna was
' Libra 2° the computation would be as follows:

Lagna (even sign) : 360°-9517° = 2513° (A)
Hora lagna (odd sign) : 652? : _ 8)

(8) - (A) = 652° - 2513° = 3819
Therefore Varnada Lagna = 12s - 3s519° = 8sll1°
(Saggitarius) .

This method 15 recommended.

4.3.15. आद्यादि स्व वर्णः॥

The Varnada dasa is the signs (in years) from the
ascendant (and other houses) to the Vamada Lagna (and
other varnadas) : :

Note : Parasara;

*“होरालग्नभयोनैया सबलाद्‌ वर्णदा दशा।।
यतूसंख्यो वर्णदो लग्नात्‌ तत्तत्संख्या क्रमणे तु॥।*'

The stronger between the Lagna and Hora Lagna shall
initiate the Varnada dasa. The Varnada dasa period of a
sign is obtained by counting from the sign to its Varnada.
For example, the ascendant at Capricorn and Hora Lagna
at Libra gives the Varnada Lagna in Saggitarius. Since
Capricorn is a Samapada (even footed) sign, count in the
reverse from it to Saggitarius to obtain the dasa as one
year(2-1). Similarly the second from Lagna is Aquarius
(11th from Aries) and the second from Hora Lagna is
Scorpio (5th from Pisces). Thus the Vamada of the second

---

## Page 384

374 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras

house is obtained by counting 6 signs (11-5) from Aries
(Aquarius is odd) to get Virgo. The Varnada dasa of
Aquarius is obtained by counting in the reverse (Sampada)
` from it to Virgo i.e. 5 year (6-1)

4.3.22. त्रि त्रि भागा: चरस्थिरोभयपर्यायात्‌॥

The Pranapada traverses one-third of the zodiac as the
ascendant traverses a sign and is added to the Sun’s longi-
tude on the basic of the three divisions- movable, fixed &
dual.

Note: (i) 'Tri-bhaga' means one third of the zodiac or
four signs as the ascendant traverses one sign. Thus the
time of birth (from Sunrise) in Vighatis should be
multiplied by 4 (or the time from sunrise in seconds be

divided by 6). This should be added to the longitude of the

Sun. If the Sun is in a movable sign, this sum becomes the
pranapada. If the Sun is in a fixed sign, add 8 signs to the
sum to obtain pranapada and if in a dual sign, and 4 signs
to the sum to obtain Pranapada.

(ii) Example: Native born at 21:14 जाए IST.: Sun Rise
: 5 `: 29414 IST Sun : 3s 21°: 14

Birth time = (21 : 14") - (5:29) = Hr 15 : 45’

(a) Birth time (Vighati) = 15.75 x 2.5 x 6 = 2362.5
Prana =2363.5 x 4 = 9450° (A) or,

(b) Birth time (seconds) = 15.75 x 3600 = 56700
Prana = 56700 + 6 = 9450° (B)

Expunging multipyes of 360°, Prana = 90° = 3s0°

---

## Page 386

376 | Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
, Pranapada = Long (Sun) + Prana = 35821०4“ + 3s0°
= 6s21°4’

Since the Sun is in a movable sign, this is the
pranapada.

4.3.23, घटिकाः षष्ठि निर्णये॥

The duration of the day is taken as sixty ghatikas to

` # the Ghatika Lagna (and Ista Ghati).

Note : (i) The birth time (in hours from Sunrise) be
~ multiplied by 2.5 to obtain the Ghati (Ista Ghati). This
should be converted to signs, degrees and added to the

` . Sun’s longitude to obtain Ghatika lagna.

0) In the example, birthtime is 15.75 hours =
15.75x2.5 = 39.375 or Ghati (39-22-33). Now, expunge
multiples of 12s from the Ghati (39.375-12 x 3 = 3.375 =
3s 11°15"). Thus the Ghatika Lagna is 7s2°19° (Sun +
Ghati = 3s21°4" + 3s511°15°) or Scorpio.

4.3.24. अशस्यैकस्य पड्म घटिकाः॥
The Bhava Lagna (also called Amsa Lagna) is five
ghatikas. : :

६

Note : The Ista Gahti be divided by 5 & converted to
signs degrees etc. and added to the longitude of the Sun to
obtain Bhava Lagna. In the example, Ista Ghati =39.375.
Therefore Bhava = 39.375/5=7.875=7s26° 15’. Thus Bhava
Lagna is in Pisces (Sunt Bhav = 3s 21°4" + 7s 26°15" =
11s 17°19").

4.3.25. एवं द्वादश पञ्च स्युः विघटिकादि क्रमेण॥

- Similarly the vighatika Lagna is obtained by increas- =
ing the Ghatikas five times and expunging multiples of 12

signs. |
: Note: The Ista ghati in the example is 39.375. Thus
ः Vighatika = 39.375 x 5 = 196.875 signs.

long life. However the strength of benefics & malefics are
to be considered before a forecast.

If the Navamsa Lagna is in the sign in the seventh

Note : (1) Dhanya = 19/12 = 7.

(n) The principle used in stanza 4.3.69-73 is that the
fith house from the Navamsa Lagna is treated as the
temporary placement of the Lord of the ascendant The
tenth house from this or the second from Navamsa Lagna
is the activity/ matter that succeeds. For example, if the
Navamsa Lagna is in the eleventh house, the fifth from it
1.6. the third house becomes the temporary placement.
Now, read the results for the ascendant Lord in the third
hous 'virtuous, fortunate etc’. The tenth house from this
will be the twelfth from ascendant. This shows success in
religious activities and final emancipation. Thus, the re-
sult, obtained are of the sign in the second.

---

## Page 396

386 | Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
(iii) Chattira Rasi

` (a) The sign occupied by the Navamsa Lagna is called
the Chattira Rasi of the Lagna.

(b) Determine the Surya Veedhi rasi from the natal
Sun sign. (Table 4.1). Count from the Arudha Lagna to
Janma Lagna (birth ascendant). Now count as many signs
from the Surya Veedhi rasi to arrive at the Chattira rasi
for Arudha Lagna .For example if the ascendant is Pisces,
Arudha Lagna 15 Saggitarius and the Sun is in Cancer, first
determine the Surya Veedhi rasi from Table 4.1. This will
be Aries. Counting from Saggitarius to Pisces we have four
sign. Now count four signs from Aries (Surya Veedhi) to
arrive at Cancer which is the Chattira rasi for the Arudha
Lagna.

Table : 4.1: Surya Veedhi Rasi

Sun Sign Surya Veedhi

Scorpio, Saggitarius Gemini
Capricorn, Aquarius

4.3.94. अंशे ग्रह बलानाम्‌॥
The strength of the planets in the divisional chart are
to be considered independantly

Note: (i) ‘Amse’ has been interpreted as divisional

chart in continuity with the preceding stanza. For example, `

if the Sun is exalted in the Rasi chart, but is in Libra in

the Sun, beeing in the 8th from AK in debility in trimsamsa

exaltation/ other strength of the Sun in the Rasi chart have
no bearing in the divisional chart which is to be considered
independantly for stanza 4.3.89-93.etc.

` (it) If Amse’ is taken as ‘degrees’ or longitude of the .

planet irrespective of signs, this stanza will mean " The
strength of the planets (to be the Atma and other Karakas)
will depend on their longitude. The highest will be the
strongest and Atmakarak etc."This interpretation is. also
correct

(iii) If ‘Amse’ is taken in the plural sence to mean the
various divisional charts, then this stanza will mean "The
strength of a planet will depend on the division it occupies
‘in the Shadvarga/ Saptavarga or other scheme”, in lines
with stanza 4.3.52. This is also correct. However the inter-
pretation given is the most relevant in the context.

4.3.95. रवि शुक्राभ्यां प्रथमम्‌ ।
! The Sun sign and Venus, shall rule the first month of
‘pregnancy.

Note: Most commentators have interpreted this stanza
as stronger between Sun or Venus. However, 1 beg to
differ on two points Firstly in stanza 4.1.1. Jaimini states
that the Sun is the Karaka for the body and since the body
is formed during pregnancy, it is the Karaka for the entire

Lal

---

## Page 401

Chapter IV Quarter III | 391

process and shall account for the development of body
` parts in ths same manner as the Moon accounts for the
maintainance of the body parts in stanzas 4.1.2. to 4.1.15.
Thus, the ten months of pregnancy are ruled by the ten
houses fron the Sun, each accounting for one month of
preganancy.

Secondly, no where has Jaimini mentioned stronger
. between the two of Sun/Venus, and it is not proper to
assume this. Instead treat the concerned sign for the month
as the bhava and the planet as the karaka for the month as
is implied under Bhyam'. Thus; for the first month, the
sign occupied by the Sun is the Bhava and Venus is the
` Karaka.

4.3.103. एवं सर्वे, रन्ध भाग्ये FAN E

In this manner the ten houses from the Sun rule th
ten months while the planets rule eight months with the
` exception of the second and the tenth. :

Note: Randhra = 22/12= 10; Bhagya 14/12 = 2.

In this stanza Jaimini states that there are no karakas for
. the second and tenth while in the stanza 4.3.96, he assigns
the karakatwa to Moon. It will be noticed that but for Venus
who is the fixed significator of father & the sperm, all other
planets are in their order of week days. Hence these are the
fixed significator of the month, However, to avoid ambiguity
between stanza 4.3.103 & 4.3.96 the karakatwa of the Moon
and all others should be shifted down one step i.e. Moon is
the karaka for the third month and so on till Ketu being the
karaka of the ninth month. Table 4.2. gives the rulership and
karakas (both fixed and natural) for the ten months of
preganancy.

` 4.3.104. लाभे च तत्र लाभयोः॥

The seventh house from Adhana lagna as well as the
second and seventh therefrom (i.e. eighth house) should be _
examined.

Note : Labha = 43/12 = 7; Tatra = 26/12 = 2.

The second seventh and eighth houses from the adhana
lagna should be examined for affliction by planets asnd
signs. The periods of the planets and signs are to be
determined from table 4.2 to indicate the month when the
problem occurs as well as the part that is damaged.

4.3.107. रन्ध वादे सौम्ये त्रिकोणे मृग वर्गाविः॥

If the Lords of the month of birth are in the tenth or
twelfth or in trines to Mercury (and afflict), the body part
indicated may be damaged/deformed.

Note: Randhra =22/12=10; Vade=84/12=12;

As the Sun ruling the fifth house of the natural zodiac
is the chief governor for the pregnancy and child birth, so
also Mercury ruling the sixth house of the natural zodiac
(2nd from 5th) is the chief governor for deformities and
miscarriages.(Hence Venus (Sperm) is debiliated in Virgo).

4.3.108. स्व त्रिंशांश: स्व नीच भवने॥
Planets placed in the 12th & 8th houses from trimsamsa
Lagna can also indicate the deformity/danger of miscarriage.

Explanatory Notes

Jaimini Maharishi has given considerable details on
the use of the Varnada dasas and their impact in the
~ divisional charts as well as the varnadas of the various
houses. This is followed by an exposition of female
horoscopy giving various combinations for Joose morals
including going to the extent of murdering spouse. These
can also be applied to male charts and natal horoscopes as
has been explained by Kalyan Verma in Saravali. The
portion pertaining to gestation period and lords etc. is quite
ingenious. These can be applied to mundane charts like
building construction, etc. with slight modifications. While

५.

---

## Page 407

` Chapter IV Quarter III ` 397

the Sun, being Deha Karak initiates the monthly dasas
from its sign position, Ketu being Grihakarak would ini-
tiate the dasas for building construction. In this manner the
dasas are to be understood. Calculation of Varnada etc
have already been explained in the first chapter, first
quarter. A few illustration on other matters are being taken
up.

4.4.1 गुणेषु गुणाः रमण्या।
The possibilty of children are seen from the fifth and
ninth houses (from the ascendant etc.)

Note : Guna = 53/12 = 5; Gunesu Guna's the fifth,
and fifth from it i.e. ninth house. Children are seen from
the 5th/9th houses from the ascendant, Arudha Lagna &
Jupiter. The fifth from Vamada Lagna is seen form their
longivity etc. Traditionally, the fifth for male, and ninth for
female charts are seen.

number of children is seen from the number of planets
aspecting/conjoining the fifth lord.

4.4.6. यथा निहरणम्‌॥ `
Similarly, draw a chart for the first menstruation and
judge the children, spouse, widowhood etc. from it.

Note : This is a standard procedure to confirm the
indications of the birth chart. Prasna Marga explaings that
if the indications of any chart constructed after birth are
contrary to a the natal chart, it is due to the misdeeds of the
person in the present birth. The chart for first menstruation
should also be examined like the natal chart

4.4.31. QUI, राहवारान्तरालश्च॥
If the full Moon is sandwiched between Rahu and Mars
in a sign, then too conception is likely.

4.4.32. शुभ वर्गे शुभ दृष्टि युतः॥
Similarly the Moon in beneficial division or with ben-
eficial aspects indicates conception.

4.4.33. अंशे मित्र भेदात्‌॥
The Moon in the Navamsa of friends indicates the pos-
sibility of conception. Co

4.4.34. स्वे नन्वे तुल्ये वा॥
4.4.35. वर्गे नवांशे AN

The Moon in the first, fourth or eighth houses both in
Rasi or Navamsa indicates the likelihood of a conception.

Note : 'Swa' is first of Lagna; Nanda=80/12=8; Tulya =
, 16/12=4

The 4th & 8th are chaturasras.

4.4.36. तत्र तत्र ज्ञानाज्ञानेषु॥ `
Inidividual pregnancies are seen after every two signs.

Note: Tatra=26/12=2; ‘Tatra Tatra’ means second to the
second or the third house. The first child is seen in the fifth
house, the second in third from fifth ie. seventh house, the
third in the third from seventh i.e. ninth house and
80 on.

4.4.37. पुत्रो मणि च रमण्याः॥
The sex of that child as male / female (of the individual
preganacies) are seen from these houses ः

4.4.39. शुभ चन्दराभ्याम्‌॥
The birth of children is seen from Mercury / Ketu or
from the ninth house from Lagna / Moon,

Note : Subha = 45/12 = 9.

4.440, स्व लग्न नाथाश्च।
The birth of children is also seen from the Lords of lagna
or third house

Note: 'Swa' 15 Lagna / Arudha Lagna; Lagna = 3. The
third house is eleventh (gains) from the fifth house.

ILLUSTRATION. |

(A) Estimating the number of children and the planets

` that will cause their birth is an important task of the astrolo- `

ger. The fifth house and its Lord should be examined first for

` conjunction and then for aspects. Similarly, the ninth attains

significance in female charts. The ability to procreate is seen -
from the fifth house and conjunction of Mercury & Venus

` could deny children. There are many such combinations which -
~ can be seen in standard texts and recent books like that of Dr.

MALE 12TH NOV. 1934
CUTTACK.

The Lagna is stronger than the Arudha Lagna.

The fifth house is Virgo unconjoined and unaspected.
The fifth Lord Mercury conjoins the Sun (debilitated),
Venus, and Jupiter in Libra indicating the birth of three
sons (Venus, Jupiter and Mercury in the order of

- decreasing longitude; Sun being debiliated is excluded). The
“native has three sons born during Rahu -Merc-Venus

(1st son) Rahu -Merc-Jup (2nd) Rahu-Ketu-Merc (3rd Son).
(Vimsottari dasa)

‘Chart 80 : Female born on 17th February 1941 at 8:25’am
IST at Delhi.

In Chart 80, the ninth house is Cancer (revese count).
. Cancer is aspected by the Sun & Mercury. The Lord Moon is
in Libra indicating the birth of sons. Moon is also aspected
by the Sun & Mercury. However, the Moon is ill placed
from the Lagna. Hence, although she had 3 pregnancies,
the first pregnancy (Moon) was lost and then two sons were
born.

The seventh house is Virgo with Rahu in it indicating
that the Lagna of spouse can be Aquarius (ruled by Rahu).
The Upapada (UL) is in Gemini and among the signs in trines
(Gemini, Aquarius, Libra) and the seventh (Saggitarius)
from it , Aquarius is the strongest with two planets and 7th
Lord Mercury. This also indicates Aquarius as the ascendant
of her husband. Her husband was born in Aquarius
ascendant. | ः

## Page 423

Chapter IV Quarter IV 413

Chart 81: Female born on 27th May,1967 at 5:25 pm IST,
Dethi Upapada: (UL) Capricorn.

Libra rises in chart 81 and the ninth house
(zodiacal count) is Gemini with Venus in it aspected
by Mars and Saturn. While Mars could indicate
difficulties in child birth, the aspect of Saturn can
be adverse especially from the sixth house indicating
a tendency to ignore children. However the presence
of Venus predominates to indicate child birth. The `
ninth Lord Mercury is in Taurus (feminine sign) with
the Sun and aspected by Moon and Ketu, indicating up
to four children (maximum) with more girls. She ha two
daughters. ` |

The Upapada is in Capricorn indicating that the 25-
- cendant of spouse could be the earthy trines (Capricorn,
Taurus or Virgo) or the seventh from Upapada (Can-
cer). Rahu is in the seventh from Ascendant (Aquarius).
The seventh Lord Mars is in Virgo ruling out Aquarius
(8th house). Her husband was born in Taurus ascendant.

## Page 424

` 414 Jaimini Maharishi’s Upadesa Sutras
` IST at Delhi.

CHART 82

Upapada (UL) : Libra.

In chart 82, Aquarius rises with the ninth house Gemini

“vacant and unaspected. The Lord Mercury joins a seven planet
constellium in Capricorn, indicating that the native can have

, up to seven children. She has two, a daughter and a son, which
is better revealed by the Saptamsa chart.

The seventh house Leo is vacant, but aspected by the
: seven planets from Capricorn. The Upapada is in Libra indi- `
cating the ascendant (Jagnanaths rule) at the early signs, Li-
bra, Aquarius or Gemini or the seventh house Aries. The hus-
band was born in Gemini ascendant. Readers will appreciate
that while Jaimini has indicated that all about spouse should
be known from upapada, some additional hints like Jagnanaths
“rule for the ascendant in trines or seventh from it are quite
- helpful. However, it should be born in mind that these are
thumb rules applicable in 80 percent of the cases.
